## 0. Build philosophy (north star)

StructureBot is built to persist. A failing result is a diagnostic signal, not a verdict. The default response to a shortcoming is to root-cause and solve it вЂ” not to work around it, lower the bar, or write off a component. "It can't be done" is a conclusion that must be earned through investigation, never assumed. Honest assessment exists to direct the fix, not to justify stopping; a caveat flags a real risk to be solved, it is not an exit. Precedent: an apparent 47% "weak local model" was a silent num_ctx truncation throttle, found only because the first verdict was refused and the config audited.

### Investigation & Audit Discipline (operationalizes the north star above)

The paragraph above is the **why** вЂ” a failing result is a diagnostic signal, not a verdict; root-cause and solve, never write off a component. This is the **how** вЂ” the protocol that keeps that principle from eroding into "the model isn't good enough." (The principle has been honored in spirit yet still defeated in practice by reaching for the model first вЂ” see the colour-the-ligand precedent below вЂ” because the *attribution map* was missing, not the resolve. This subsection is that map.)

**Pipeline attribution вЂ” required before any cause is named.** Route a gap to the subsystem that PRODUCED it, which is the same as routing to where the FIX lives:
- **Translator (LLM)** вЂ” the ONLY path where the model's own output is actually used. Reproduce `translator.translate(...)` in isolation: if it is correct, the model is exonerated and the bug is downstream.
- **Router** вЂ” for **op-class commands (color, representation вЂ” any handler that regenerates the command from raw English)** the ROUTER builds the final command and the translator's output is DISCARDED (`tool_router.route()` clears it; `_run_color` / `_run_representation` rebuild it from the user's English via the shared op-class target resolver). An accuracy/scoping complaint there is a ROUTER fix, not a model fix вЂ” the translator was likely already right.
- **Guards** вЂ” deterministic post-processing (`_sanitize_zone_syntax`, `_scope_chain_refs_to_macromolecule`, the emission guard).
- **Config / environment** вЂ” versions, GPU-vs-CPU placement, context window (`num_ctx`), timeouts, dependencies.
- **The measurement instrument** вЂ” a benchmark/audit run against a broken pipeline mis-attributes config/code failures as model failures; verify the instrument scores the true end-to-end output and is itself sound before trusting its verdict.

**"It's the model" is reached LAST** вЂ” not because the model is never the constraint, but because here it has repeatedly been the *wrong first guess*: the 47% "weak model" was a silent `num_ctx=8192` truncation throttle (config); the Ollama-on-CPU and 0.24-vs-0.30 version misses were config; the "colour the ligand white" failure was the op-class router regenerating the command from English (code) вЂ” the translator emitted `color ligand white` correctly. Even when the model genuinely IS the constraint, that is a diagnostic directing a model-level solution (prompt, few-shot, decomposition, a stronger local model, `num_ctx`/quantization tuning) вЂ” never a write-off or a stop.

**Objectivity standard вЂ” an audit/benchmark must meet all five, or it is not trustworthy:**
1. **Ground-truth, end-to-end** вЂ” score the real pipeline's final output (post-router, what reaches ChimeraX) against curated expected outputs; falsifiable and re-runnable.
2. **Subsystem attribution** вЂ” report WHERE the gap is (translator / router / guard / config / instrument), i.e. which fix it routes to.
3. **Empirical-exhaustive, not predicted** вЂ” check the whole surface (every env, handler, tool), never only where a problem is expected.
4. **Adversarial** вЂ” probe with wide, varied, partly-randomized real inputs to find divergence from intent, not to confirm health.
5. **Coverage honesty** вЂ” report what was NOT examined and the boundary of what was seen; "no findings" never means "nothing there."

**Standing rule.** Future audit/benchmark briefs reference this section and must satisfy the standard; one that cannot state its coverage boundary, cannot attribute failures to a subsystem, or checked only where a problem was expected is incomplete and is to be redone. Behavioral observation вЂ” real use, tracing concrete failures to root cause вЂ” is the highest-value signal and outranks any checklist audit.

**ChimeraX command-form discipline (2026-06-17).** Before changing the FORM of any ChimeraX command the code emits (adding/removing a `target`, a keyword, a default), grep the codebase for existing usage AND verified-notes first вЂ” ChimeraX has documented silent-success gaps where a command runs without error but has NO visible effect. Precedent: a bare `transparency #N <pct>` (no `target`) silently no-ops on cartoons in 1.11.1 вЂ” already documented inline in `_run_conformer_comparison`; an op-class change dropped `target acs` to a bare command and reintroduced exactly that silent failure because the existing note wasn't consulted. A unit test must pin the REQUIRED command form (e.g. "target includes b+c"), not merely assert "a command was emitted" вЂ” a test edited to match wrong code catches nothing.

### Invariant вЂ” LLM translation is LOCAL-ONLY (2026-06-14)

**All natural-language understanding runs on a LOCAL model (Ollama / `qwen3:8b`) вЂ” there is no Claude/Anthropic path, no API key, and no external-network or server-side-state dependency in the translate/classify pipeline.** A remote LLM for translation is a disqualifying vulnerability here (external dependency + server-side state + the data leaving the machine), so it was removed entirely: the `ClaudeBackend`, the backend-selection switch (`TRANSLATOR_BACKEND`/`make_backend` runtime selection), the API-key handling, the one-way fallback/usage-cap latch, and the `anthropic` SDK are all gone. The only network call in the translate path is `localhost:11434` (Ollama); Ollama is therefore a hard REQUIRED dependency (the preflight blocks on it вЂ” no fallback exists). **В§0's "LLM infers intent" rule is UNCHANGED** вЂ” the LLM still infers/clarifies intent and never writes tool syntax; it is simply *always local now*. (`make_backend` survives as a benchmark-only shim that returns the Ollama backend and *raises* on `"claude"` вЂ” the Claude eval arm is retired; its historical Claude-vs-local numbers are preserved in В§7.)

### Named build rule вЂ” Intent/Render separation

**"The LLM infers and clarifies intent; it never writes tool syntax."**

For any operation class where the set of valid outputs is known and finite, the LLM returns a canonical INTENT LABEL from a closed vocabulary вЂ” it never emits the tool-specific syntax directly. A separate deterministic render layer owns the syntax (single source of truth, probe-verified). This decoupling means: (a) miscategorization is recoverable via the 3-tier resolution pipeline (alias в†’ LLM classifier в†’ graceful miss), (b) malformed syntax for covered ops is structurally impossible, (c) the LLM's role stays what it is good at вЂ” understanding natural language вЂ” not what it is bad at (memorizing exact API calling conventions).

**3-tier resolution pipeline:** (1) Deterministic alias match (substring, instant, no LLM); (2) LLM constrained classifier (`make_llm_classify_fn()` вЂ” returns ONLY a label from the valid set, "uncovered", or "none"; never prose or syntax); (3) Graceful miss (lists the known intents, asks the user to rephrase вЂ” never guesses). Tier 1 covers the common phrases; Tier 2 handles paraphrases; Tier 3 ensures the system never silently does the wrong thing.

**LLM classifier backend:** the classifier uses the **LOCAL Ollama model only** (no Claude path вЂ” local-only, per the invariant above). The Ollama call places `think: false` at the **TOP LEVEL** of the request JSON вЂ” NOT inside `options{}`. For qwen3 models, `think` inside `options` is silently ignored and the model generates a thinking block that consumes `num_predict` tokens в†’ empty response в†’ classified as miss. With the fix, `num_predict` is 60 (not 30) to avoid truncation on longer intent keys. The Claude API monthly cap no longer kills the classification tier.

**Per-target representation snapshot + undo intent (2026-06-08):** before executing any non-undo render, `ToolRouter._snapshot_repr()` probes the current atoms/cartoon/style state via `runscript` and stores restore commands in `_repr_snapshots[spec]`. `view.undo_representation` intent ("strip it back", "undo that", "put it back", etc.) executes the stored restore commands and clears the snapshot. No prior snapshot в†’ graceful miss (not a free-translation guess).

**Noun-floor gate + authoritative alias (2026-06-08 structural fix; surface tier revised same day вЂ” FIX 2):** `detect_category_phrase()` now uses two structural tiers instead of a literal-phrase list. (1a) Authoritative alias match вЂ” `resolve_alias()` positive в†’ always representation (catches "strip it back", "undo that", etc. regardless of other words in the phrase). The old phrase-list veto (`_REP_SURFACE_NEGATIVE`) is **removed**; "surface" no longer resolves via a bare alias, so there is nothing to veto. (1b) Conservative noun-floor вЂ” unambiguous rep nouns (cartoon, ribbon, spacefill, stick/sticks, ball/balls, wire/wireframe, mesh, licorice, cpk) are always flagged; ambiguous nouns вЂ” atom/atoms, sphere/spheres, **and now surface/surfaces** вЂ” flag ONLY when a display verb is also present (one shared verb set: show, hide, remove, display, style, reveal, add, apply, ditch, lose, drop, "get rid of", "no more"). Bare-token "surface"/"surfaces" as the whole input в†’ treated as rep. Single-word verbs are matched on word boundaries (`\bвЂ¦\b`) so "drop" inside "hydrophobic" and "lose" inside "closely" do NOT false-fire; multi-word verbs ("get rid of") substring-match safely. This is structural вЂ” "lose the sticks", "get rid of the balls on chain A", "ditch the surface", "show the surface" are caught deterministically; "fold the top design", "how many atoms", "binding surface", "the surface of the dimer", "hydrophobic surface patch", "surface contacts between chains" are NOT over-blocked (they free-translate to a biology/render answer instead of silently no-op'ing as they did under the old veto).

**Emission guard at execution choke-point (В§0 invariant; origin-scoped вЂ” FIX 1, 2026-06-08):** `main._execute_commands(commands, origin=...)` runs an emission guard before calling `bridge.run_commands()`. The guard fires **only for `origin="translation"`** (the default вЂ” free-translated commands from the translator/error-fix path). Any representation-shaped command (hide/show with #spec and atoms/cartoons/sphere/surface targets; style #spec sphere/stick/ball; surface/~surface #spec; bare cartoon/ribbon/spacefill with #spec) from translation is **blocked with an error** вЂ” it never reaches ChimeraX. Three execution paths, three trust levels: (a) the **render layer** (`_run_representation()`) bypasses `_execute_commands()` entirely; (b) **tool-generated viz** (ColabFold cartoon, double-mutant cartoon/show/style/label/distance) calls `_execute_commands(viz_cmds, origin="tool_viz")` вЂ” a trusted origin that is guard-exempt; (c) **free-translation** (`origin="translation"`) is the only guarded origin. The structural invariant holds: even if the category gate misses a phrase and the translator emits a representation command, it cannot execute вЂ” while legitimate tool viz is never falsely blocked. Note this is an **origin** parameter, not a `skip_guard=True` bypass switch вЂ” a tool cannot opt OUT of guarding; it declares WHAT it is, and the guard policy is owned centrally. Live-confirmed 2026-06-08: double-mutant scan ran 43 viz commands / 0 blocked; free-translated `cartoon #1` (from "binding surface") blocked as expected.

**Pre-translate interception:** covered operations bypass `translate()` entirely вЂ” `detect_category_phrase()` in `_handle_request()` routes to the representation tool before the translator is called, avoiding both the latency and the risk of the LLM writing syntax for a covered op.

**Post-command verify guard:** after executing render-layer commands, `_probe_atom_count()` (via `runscript`) confirms the structural state changed as expected. A False verify is a warning; a None verify (probe failed) is a safe no-op.

**Error detection hardening:** `_ERROR_PREFIXES` in `chimerax_bridge.py` now includes `"Expected"` to catch `"Expected a collection of one of 'atoms', 'bonds'вЂ¦"` вЂ” previously these were silently passed as success. Any response matching an error prefix is `FAILED`, not `вњ“`.

**Current scope:** the viewer-representation AND color op-classes are both LANDED (representation: cartoon/spacefill/sticks/ball-and-stick/surface/hide-atoms/hide-cartoon/hide-surface/show-atoms/undo-representation; color: by-chain/by-element/by-heteroatom/rainbow/by-attribute/solid), both on the shared op-class target resolver (`_resolve_opclass_target` вЂ” see the Investigation & Audit Discipline subsection above). The remaining op-class migration (selection, etc.) is the documented next phase вЂ” see В§9.

---

## 1. Project Overview

StructureBot is a Windows-native natural-language interface for UCSF ChimeraX 1.11.1, running on Python 3.14 (main venv) with a GPU/ML delegation layer in Python 3.12 (venv312). Users type free-text biology requests ("suggest mutations to improve solubility of chain A, avoiding interfaces") into a PySide6 GUI (or a Rich-console REPL via `--console`); the system translates those requests **locally** via Ollama (`qwen3:8b` on the RTX 5070 Ti вЂ” LOCAL-ONLY by design, no external-network/server-side dependency; see В§0), routes them through a pipeline of computational bridges (CamSol, ESM-2, ProteinMPNN, PyRosetta, DynaMut2, disulfide/proline/glycan/cavity/salt-bridge/double-mutant analysers), and executes the resulting ChimeraX commands via the ChimeraX REST API on port 60001. The application also supports a `--script` batch mode and session persistence via `session.json`.

---

## 2. Architecture

### Data Flow

```
User input (Rich REPL or --script file)
  в”‚
  в–ј
main.py / StructureBot
  в”‚  1. config.load_env_file()  в†ђ loads .env.local FIRST
  в”‚  2. CommandTranslator.translate()
  в”‚     в””в”Ђ LOCAL Ollama (qwen3:8b @ localhost:11434) вЂ” no external network
  в”‚        Block 1: STATIC prompt (cached, ephemeral cache_control)
  в”‚        Block 2: DYNAMIC session context (uncached, changes per turn)
  в”‚  3. ToolRouter.route()      в†ђ augments result, no execution
  в”‚     Intent overrides (in order): validate_ddg в†’ colabfold в†’ proline в†’ mpnn_esmfold
  в”‚     в†’ glycan_positions в†’ netnglyc в†’ glycan в†’ salt_bridge в†’ cavity в†’ double_mutant
  в”‚     в†’ mutation_scan (fallback, last)
  в”‚  4. User confirmation / auto-proceed countdown
  в”‚  5. ChimeraXBridge.run_commands()  в†ђ initial viz commands
  в”‚  6. ToolRouter.execute()    в†ђ computational pipeline
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ CamsolBridge         в†ђ local algorithm, no network
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ EsmBridge            в†ђ delegates to venv312 subprocess
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ESMFoldBridge        в†ђ delegates to venv312 subprocess
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ RosettaBridge        в†ђ DynaMut2 API or WSL2 PyRosetta
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ MutationScanner      в†ђ orchestrates CamSol+ESM+Rosetta
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ DoubleMutantBridge   в†ђ DynaMut2 prediction_mm + optional PyRosetta
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ DisulfideBridge      в†ђ BioPython + ESM + DynaMut2
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ProlineBridge        в†ђ BioPython + ESM
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ GlycanBridge         в†ђ BioPython + ESM + NetNGlyc API
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ AssemblyAnalyser     в†ђ RCSB API + ChimeraX zone-select
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ SaltBridgeBridge     в†ђ BioPython + FreeSASA
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ CavityBridge         в†ђ BioPython ShrakeRupley
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ProteinMPNNBridge    в†ђ subprocess: protein_mpnn_run.py
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ColabFoldBridge      в†ђ WSL2 ~/colabfold_env worker (AF2, remote MSA)
  в”‚     в””в”Ђ RFdiffusionBridge    в†ђ вњ… ACTIVATED 2026-06-12 (wsl.exeв†’RFDIFFUSION_PYTHON; ~/rfdiffusion_env, dgl sm_120)
  в”‚  7. ChimeraXBridge.run_commands()  в†ђ viz commands from tools
  в”‚  8. SessionState.add_to_history()
  в”‚
  в–ј
ChimeraX REST API  (http://127.0.0.1:60001/run)
```

### Two-Venv Architecture

| Venv | Python | Purpose |
|------|--------|---------|
| `venv/` | 3.14 | Main process: PySide6 (GUI), Rich, BioPython, requests (translation via the local Ollama HTTP API вЂ” `anthropic` UNINSTALLED, local-only), all bridges |
| `venv312/` | 3.12 | GPU/ML delegation: torch 2.11.0+cu128 (RTX 5070 Ti, sm_120), ESM-2 inference, ESMFold inference |

GPU ESM/ESMFold/ThermoMPNN inference runs in the **venv312 subprocess** (cu128, sm_120); the main venv delegates to it via JSON I/O (`--input`/`--output` temp files), and the worker scripts have **no project imports** (only `torch`/`transformers`/`esm`/stdlib). The main venv's **own** torch is the **CPU build (`2.12.0+cpu`)** вЂ” imported lazily by `esm_bridge` ONLY for the in-process ESM fallback (used when the venv312 subprocess is unavailable; it runs on CPU by design). **Audit remediation (2026-06-13):** a prior `torch 2.12.0+cu126` was installed here вЂ” `cuda.is_available()` returned True but it is **NOT sm_120-compatible** (built в‰¤sm_90), the exact "looks-connected-but-can't-GPU" trap; it was replaced with `+cpu`, removing the silent-CPU trap and reclaiming ~3.9 GB. The main venv was never the GPU path.

### WSL2 Layer (PyRosetta)

When `ROSETTA_BACKEND=local`, `RosettaBridge._run_rosetta_local()` builds a standalone Python worker script as an f-string, writes it to a Windows temp file, translates the path to `/mnt/c/...` form, and runs it via `WSLBridge.run_python_script()` в†’ `wsl.exe --distribution Ubuntu-24.04 --exec bash -c "{PYROSETTA_PYTHON} '{wsl_path}'"`. Results are returned as a JSON file at `/tmp/rosetta_ddg_{hash}.json`, copied back to Windows via `wsl.exe`. Same pattern applies to `DoubleMutantBridge._run_pair_pyrosetta()` for close pairs.

**Worker script constraints** (critical, applies to ALL worker scripts):
- No project imports вЂ” completely standalone
- Communicates only via JSON files in `/tmp/`
- All subprocess calls in `wsl_bridge.py` use `stdin=subprocess.DEVNULL` and `creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW`

### Unified front-end вЂ” RequestEngine + Presenter (2026-06-13)

StructureBot has ONE orchestration core driven by TWO interchangeable front-ends:

- **The GUI is the default** вЂ” `python main.py` launches the unified PySide6 GUI (`gui_app.StructureBotWindow`): a conversation pane + command box over the sequence-model tabs, in one window beside ChimeraX. It is **self-launching** вЂ” it brings up ChimeraX (REST 60001) and Ollama (`ollama serve`, a managed background service) itself, renders the вњ“ checklist to the pane, and offers session restore as a GUI prompt.
- **`python main.py --console`** runs the original REPL вЂ” now the **parity oracle + debug fallback**, behaviourally identical on the same engine. PySide6 is imported lazily so console-only use never requires it. `--script FILE` also uses the console path.
- **`RequestEngine` (request_engine.py)** is UI-agnostic: it performs ALL input/output through a **`Presenter`** (presenter.py). `ConsolePresenter` is the oracle (verbatim Rich console); `QtPresenter` (qt_presenter.py) renders to the pane and, critically, runs on a **worker thread** вЂ” its OUTPUT methods marshal to the UI thread via queued signals and its BLOCKING input methods (`ask_clarification`/`confirm`/`ask_edit`/`ask_yes_no`) block the worker on a `queue.Queue` while the UI thread stays live. This worker-thread-blocking pattern is what lets the engine stay **straight-line** (no resumable state machine).
- **`engine.dispatch(text, presenter)`** is the single shared input entry both front-ends use (semicolon chaining + the bypass-LLM fast-paths + `handle_request`).
- **В§0 (LLM-infers-intent / Intent-Render separation) is UNCHANGED by this move** вЂ” the unification relocated only the I/O surface; translation, routing, the intent registries, and the emission guard are untouched.
- **The earlier two-process / IPC model is RETIRED** вЂ” there is **no** `SeqEditorManager`, **no** `QLocalServer`/socket IPC, and **no** `--model` child-spawn. The seq-editor's value (chains-as-tabs: `show_model`/`load_model`/`_focus_model`/`_LoadModelWorker`) is hosted **in-process** in the GUI; "focus the new model's tab after an open" is now the in-process structure-state hook driven by the bridge's real `_opened_model_id`.

---

## 3. Module Registry

| File | Class / Key Functions | Status | Notes |
|------|----------------------|--------|-------|
| `intent_registry.py` | `IntentDef`, `IntentRegistry`, `_probe_atom_count()`, `make_llm_classify_fn()`, `VIEWER_REGISTRY`, `COLOR_REGISTRY`, `extract_named_color()`, `_color_category_floor()`, `_CATEGORY_TRIGGERS` | вњ… Complete | **Intent/Render separation framework (В§0 named build rule).** Core dataclass: `IntentDef(name, category, aliases, render_fn, description, verify_fn)`. `IntentRegistry` provides: `register(intent_def)`, `resolve(text, llm_classify_fn=None)` в†’ `(key, method)` where method в€€ `{"alias","llm","miss"}`; `render(key, spec)` в†’ `List[str]` (deterministic command list, single source of truth); `verify(key, spec, bridge)` в†’ `Optional[bool]`; `detect_category_phrase(text)` (pre-translate interception guard); `graceful_miss_message(text, category)` (lists all registered intents for the category); `list_intent_keys(category)` (for the LLM classifier prompt). `_probe_atom_count(spec, bridge)` queries `m.atoms.displays.sum()` via `runscript` (file-based, avoids REST truncation). **`make_llm_classify_fn()` (2026-06-08 hardened):** factory returns a `(text, labels) в†’ Optional[str]` classifier. **LOCAL-ONLY (2026-06-14): calls Ollama directly** вЂ” the `_backend=="claude"` branch and the `_claude_capped` latch were removed with the Claude path; URL fallback uses `config.OLLAMA_BASE_URL`. The Ollama call places `think: false` at TOP LEVEL (not inside `options{}`); `num_predict=60`. Returns a valid intent key, "uncovered" (representation-category but no specific match в†’ graceful miss), or "none" (not a representation request в†’ graceful miss) вЂ” NEVER syntax. `_CATEGORY_TRIGGERS["view"]` вЂ” broader trigger phrases for pre-translate interception (2026-06-08: expanded with `"all spheres"`, `"all atoms"`, and undo triggers `"strip it back"`, `"undo that"`, `"put it back"`, etc.); false positives resolve to graceful miss, NEVER free-translation. **`VIEWER_REGISTRY`** вЂ” pre-populated `IntentRegistry` with **10** viewer intents, aliases probe-verified against ChimeraX 1.11.1: `view.cartoon_only` (`hide {spec} atoms` + `show {spec} cartoons` + `~surface {spec}`); `view.spacefill` (`show {spec} atoms` + `style {spec} sphere`); `view.sticks` (`show {spec} atoms` + `style {spec} stick`); `view.ball_and_stick` (`show {spec} atoms` + `style {spec} ball`); `view.surface` (`surface {spec}`); `view.hide_atoms` (`hide {spec} atoms` вЂ” NOT `hide {spec} sphere`); `view.hide_cartoon` (`hide {spec} cartoons`); `view.hide_surface` (`~surface {spec}`); `view.show_atoms` (`show {spec} atoms`); **`view.undo_representation`** (aliases: "strip it back", "undo that", "put it back", etc.; render_fn returns [] вЂ” execution handled specially in `_run_representation()`). **Verify guards** use pattern `(lambda n: None if n is None else (n == 0))(probe_result)` so a failed probe (n=None) is a safe None, not False. **`tool_router._run_representation()`** is the integration point: does the 3-tier resolution, snapshots before rendering, executes render-layer commands via bridge, handles undo, runs verify, returns `ToolStepResult`. **`main.py` pre-translate interception:** `detect_category_phrase()` check fires before `translate()`, so covered ops never reach the translator. **`chimerax_bridge._ERROR_PREFIXES`** extended with `"Expected"` to catch `"Expected a collection of one of 'atoms', 'bonds'вЂ¦"`. 148 tests in `tests/test_intent_registry.py`. **COLOR op-class (2026-06-09, Priority 0.5 вЂ” SECOND op-class on this framework):** `COLOR_REGISTRY` = `IntentRegistry` with 6 color intents, syntax probe-verified spec-FIRST against ChimeraX 1.11.1: `color.by_chain` (`color {spec} bychain`), `color.by_element` (`color {spec} byelement`), `color.by_heteroatom` (`color {spec} byhetero`), `color.rainbow` (`rainbow {spec}`), `color.by_attribute` (`color byattribute bfactor {spec} palette blue:white:red` вЂ” bfactor ONLY; hydrophobicity is not a built-in attr), `color.solid` (`color {spec} {named}`, resolved via `extract_named_color()` not alias). **Conservative gate** `_color_category_floor()`: requires an explicit color verb (`color/colour/recolor/вЂ¦`) or `rainbow` AND no sub-chain selection qualifier (`_COLOR_COMPLEX_RE`: residue type/range, named region, property) вЂ” so "color the proline residues" / "color the binding pocket" fall through to free-translation (the op-class targets only a whole chain or whole model). `detect_category_phrase(text, "color")` gates on the floor ONLY (color scheme aliases like "by chain"/"bfactor" are common non-color substrings в†’ NOT treated as authoritative, unlike viewer). `make_llm_classify_fn(registry=, task_block=)` generalised (viewer default unchanged; `_COLOR_TASK_BLOCK` for color). **`tool_router._run_color()`** is the integration point вЂ” parses target (whole chain / whole model; "each/every/all chain" в†’ whole model), resolves scheme-alias в†’ solid(named color) в†’ LLM в†’ graceful miss, renders, then reuses `translator._scope_chain_refs_to_macromolecule` so chain colors never bleed onto ligand/solvent/ions (the payoff bug). **Emission-guard extension to color DEFERRED** (false-block risk; tools emit `color bychain` in viz). Color undo DEFERRED. 66 tests in `tests/test_color_intent.py` (incl. real-`main._handle_request` integration). Live-verified on 1HSG: `color chain A red` в†’ `color (#1/A & ~ligand & ~solvent & ~ions) red`, probe solvent_red=0/ligand_red=0; paraphrase в†’ resolution=llm (Ollama). |

| `rosetta_bridge.py` | `RosettaBridge`, `_select_backend()`, `_run_command_*` (DynaMut2), `_run_rosetta_local()`, `resolve_rosetta_workers()`, `mutation_seed()`, `count_pdb_residues()`, `worker_footprint_mb()`, `per_mutation_sec()` | вљ пёЏ Magnitude bias | **Estimate-honesty fix (2026-06-09):** `count_pdb_residues(pdb)` counts the FULL pose (all chains); `worker_footprint_mb(n)` = pose-size-scaled per-worker RAM (FIX 2) so `_run_rosetta_local` caps the pool by ACTUAL pose size (2HHB tetramer в†’ 6 workers not 8, no swap); `per_mutation_sec(n)` = super-linear per-mutation cost calibrated to measured anchors (used by the tool_router estimate). **WT-relax accounting:** 1 global WT relax (cached/shared via fork COW) + 1 **symmetric** WT re-relax PER mutation inside `_score_one` (the 2Г— deep-tier cost вЂ” deliberate paired variance reduction, NOT a redundant recompute; removable only by switching to asymmetric single-shared-WT ddG в†’ now an explicit opt-in). **Asymmetric basis + large-pose estimate guard (2026-06-09):** `_run_rosetta_local(ddg_basis=)` вЂ” the worker `_score_one` runs the symmetric paired WT re-relax by default, or scores against the cached global WT when `ddg_basis="asymmetric"` (~2Г— faster, noisier, labelled). `parallel_efficiency(n_res)` (=1.0 в‰¤ the 2HHB anchor, REF/n above it) feeds the tool_router estimate so large complexes don't over-credit parallel speedup (biased high). 4 backends (dynamut2/empirical/pyrosetta-stub/local-WSL2). **Deep-tier parallelization (FIX D, Priority 1, 2026-06-09):** `_run_rosetta_local(num_workers=)` now runs the independent per-mutation FastRelax units through a **stdlib `multiprocessing.Pool` INSIDE the single WSL2 worker** (`get_context("fork")` в†’ children inherit the imported PyRosetta + the cached WT-relaxed pose copy-on-write; one wsl.exe spawn, serial fallback on pool error). **Pure speedup, IDENTICAL results:** every mutation's FastRelax RNG is seeded **deterministically** via `mutation_seed(base_seed, key, traj)` (sha256 of `(ROSETTA_BASE_SEED, key, t)`) вЂ” independent of worker id/order, so parallel output == serial output (and N=1 is now reproducible; previously system-seeded вЂ” ranking/sign unaffected either way). Pool size = `resolve_rosetta_workers(configured, physical_cores, mem_budget, per_worker)` = `min(ROSETTA_MAX_WORKERS, physical_coresв€’2, wsl_mem/footprint)`, default **8 = i9-14900HX P-cores** (NOT the 32 logical threads вЂ” E-cores/HT/single-channel DDR5/140 W throttle). Applies to BOTH the scan deep tier and `validate_ddg` (both call `_run_rosetta_local`). Live baseline that motivated it: 2HHB "scan the interface residues" ran 141-residue chain-A FastRelax SINGLE-THREADED (~1 h, ~23 cores idle). See В§4 config rows. 4 backends (dynamut2/empirical/pyrosetta-stub/local-WSL2). **DynaMut2 single parser fixed** вЂ” handles current status-based API (`status` DONE/RUNNING/ERROR), robust float cast of `prediction`, raises (never silent 0.0) on ERROR. **Local PyRosetta path hardened**: `pose_from_file` validation + `.pdb`-extension/`pose_from_pdb` fallback; whole-batch failure в†’ per-mutation **empirical fallback** (not all-zero); each value carries **`ddg_source`** (`pyrosetta`/`empirical`). **Tiered multi-trajectory ddG**: `_run_rosetta_local(num_trajectories=, relax_cycles=)` runs N independent relax+score trajectories per mutation (per-trajectory RNG seed when N>1), aggregates by **median** (`_aggregate_ddg_trajectories`), reports **MAD spread** + **`ddg_confidence`** (`_ddg_confidence_label`); WSL timeout scales by NГ—cycles. Defaults (N=1, cycles=3) = production single-trajectory, unchanged. **Protocol = manual symmetric FastRelax + torsion-space `ref2015` (`:1449-1464`), NOT the `cartesian_ddg` app / `ref2015_cart`; reported "kcal/mol" is a raw REU delta with no conversion вЂ” magnitudes are UNCALIBRATED (2.94 doesn't apply; ranking/sign reliable). See В§7.** **`validate_ddg()`** = high-accuracy tier (ROSETTA_VALIDATION_TRAJECTORIES/CYCLES) with a non-calibrated disclosure. Path validated for ranking (T4 rв‰€+0.49, sign 100%); **validation-tier 2LZM panel (N=5 Г— 8+8 cycles, median, 2026-05-30): RMSE 2.73, MAE 2.59, r +0.50, sign 90% вЂ” meets all revised thresholds (r>0.3, RMSE<4.0, sign>=60%)**, roughly halving single-traj RMSE (5.23в†’2.73). Magnitudes now tighter but still approximate (~В±2.7 kcal/mol; gain is in magnitude, not ranking). **Those panel numbers were measured with `ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS=true` (strip), which вЂ” reverted 2026-05-31 вЂ” is again the default, so they describe the DEFAULT path. Preserve-waters (`False`) is now opt-in, validated only on buried-water target T26A (+3.80 shift, sign corrected); preserve-path panel behaviour is unmeasured.** See В§7/В§8. **`relax_and_score(pdb_path, relax_cycles=3)`** (added for validate-design): FastRelax + `ref2015` total/per-residue/`fa_rep` on an ARBITRARY structure (NO mutation) via the same WSL2 worker building blocks в†’ `{total_reu, per_residue_density, fa_rep, clash_ok, converged, relaxed_pdb}`; returns a dict, never raises; **does NOT touch the ddG path** (backward-compatible). Live-validated (HP36: в€’88.4 REU, 36 res) |

| `mutation_scanner.py` | `MutationScanner`, `combined_score()`, `effective_weights()` | вњ… Complete (tiered + scoped 2026-06-09) | CamSol+ESM+Rosetta pipeline; deep-tier combined score `0.5Г—(-ddG) + 0.3Г—camsol_delta + 0.2Г—esm_tolerance`; Pro/Cys exclusion; interface protection. `_run_rosetta_batch` returns `(ddg_scores, ddg_source, ddg_spread, ddg_confidence)`; spread/confidence threaded into scan results + the summary table (scans are single-trajectory в†’ confidence "single-trajectory"). **Triageв†’validate tiering (Priority 1, 2026-06-09):** `scan()` gains `run_rosetta: bool` + `include_positions: Optional[List[int]]`. **Fast/default tier (`run_rosetta=False`)** = CamSol + ESM only вЂ” **`_run_rosetta_batch` (the only WSL2/PyRosetta spawn) is NOT called**; ddG is reported as `None` ("not computed (opt in with 'rosetta')") вЂ” **never a fake 0.0** вЂ” and the score is **renormalised** by `effective_weights(use_ddg=False)` (drops `_W_DDG=0.50`, rescales `0.30/0.20 в†’ 0.6/0.4`; structured so ThermoMPNN/RaSP can join the fast tier with another renormalise). **Deep tier (`run_rosetta=True`)** runs the existing Rosetta path. **Assignable scope (`include_positions`):** `_identify_candidates` scans ONLY the named positions and **bypasses the CamSol/ESM pre-filter** within scope (raises the candidate cap to cover them all); empty scope в†’ `[]` (caller errors, no full-chain fallback). `_recommendation`/`_generate_summary`/the router one-liner handle `ddg=None`. Tiering POLICY (scope parse, tier triggers, estimate) lives in `tool_router`; `scan()`'s own default stays `run_rosetta=True` for backward-compatible direct callers. **Coverage + lossless data model (2026-06-09):** `scan()` gains `rosetta_shortlist_k` (None = FULL grid default вЂ” Rosetta on every candidate; int = SHORTLIST top-K by fast score, the rest RETAINED as `not_computed`, never dropped) and `ddg_basis` ("symmetric" default / "asymmetric"). The candidate-generation 20-cap is REMOVED (default `max_candidates=None`) в†’ the full positionsГ—`candidates_per_pos` grid is generated and CamSol/ESM-scored (lossless; in-chat display still summarises top-N). **Every result record is now keyed by `key`=(from,pos,to) and carries `ddg_basis`, `tier` ("fast"/"deep"), `fast_score`, and the existing per-measure fields** вЂ” substrate for the future Excel export + cross-layer aggregate scoring; deferred candidates get explicit `not_computed` markers, never 0.0/blank. **ThermoMPNN fast-tier voter (2026-06-09):** `scan(run_thermompnn=True)` calls `_run_thermompnn` in the fast pass в†’ per-candidate `thermompnn_ddg`/`thermompnn_source` added to each record (chain-aware key). `present_voters_score(rosetta_ddg, thermompnn_ddg, camsol, esm, вЂ¦)` renormalises over the voters PRESENT вЂ” both ddG voters absent в†’ exactly 0.6В·camsol+0.4В·esm (graceful == pre-ThermoMPNN, byte-for-byte). Keep-both (C): Rosetta + ThermoMPNN are independent voters (learned GNN vs physics relax) вЂ” both retained when present so their agreement feeds the future aggregate-confidence layer. **Residue-identity fix (2026-06-09):** the candidate identity is now the **author resnum (+chain)**, not the sequence index. `scan()` builds the coordinate-ordered residue spine (`ordered_chain_residues`), uses the coordinate sequence for CamSol/ESM (so seqindexв†”resnum is exact), and each record carries `resnum`/`icode` (identity в†’ Rosetta/ThermoMPNN/scope/viz/display, via the `position` field) + `seqindex` (derived в†’ CamSol/ESM). **Fixes a pre-existing SHIPPED bug** where `candidate["position"]` (1-based seqindex) was treated as the author resnum by scope, the candidate key, viz, AND the gold-tier Rosetta path (`pdb2pose`) вЂ” silently wrong on any non-1-start/gapped chain; masked because all prior structures were 1-based-contiguous. Scope ("residues 30-45" = AUTHOR 30-45), Rosetta (`_run_rosetta_batch` passes resnum), and viz now address by author resnum. Legacy fallback (no PDB) keeps resnum==seqindex. **RaSP physics-proxy voter + AXIS-AWARE handoff (2026-06-10):** `scan(run_rasp=True)` calls `_run_rasp` в†’ per-candidate `rasp_ddg`/`rasp_source`. `present_voters_score` is now AXIS-AWARE: PHYSICS is ONE slot = **Rosetta if computed for that candidate, ELSE RaSP** (the proxy) вЂ” Rosetta and RaSP NEVER both vote (RaSP is a Rosetta surrogate, so it HANDS OFF per candidate, no additive double-count). When Rosetta is present, RaSP's score contribution в†’ 0 but its value is RETAINED and the **`rasp_minus_rosetta` proxy-QC delta** is stored; records also carry `physics_source` (rosetta\|rasp\|not_computed). ThermoMPNN (ML/static axis), CamSol (solubility), ESM (fitness) unchanged. `RASP_WEIGHT`/`w_rasp` are PROVISIONAL вЂ” the В§9 aggregate-weighting benchmark (independence Г— confidence) calibrates the physics-axis weight later (proxy < real); the handoff MECHANISM is what's built now. Live-verified: non-1-start chain в†’ RaSP 12/12 mapped, cross-source identity holds; deep candidate в†’ physics=Rosetta, RaSP retained + delta stored; RaSP-disabled scan == pre-RaSP byte-for-byte. **DynaMut2 DYNAMICS-axis voter (2026-06-10):** `scan(run_dynamut2=True)` calls `_run_dynamut2` on the DEEP candidate set (rides the deep opt-in; remote API в†’ SPARSE, capped by `DYNAMUT2_MAX_CANDIDATES`, top-N by fast score, rest dynamics not_computed), CONCURRENT with Rosetta (a thread вЂ” wall в‰€ max(rosetta, dynamut2), remote I/O vs local CPU). `present_voters_score` gains a DYNAMICS slot that is **INDEPENDENT вЂ” always counted when present, NEVER zeroed/handed off (the inverse of the RaSP handoff)**; records carry `dynamut2_ddg`/`dynamut2_source`. SIGN-NORMALISED via the SHARED `rosetta_bridge.normalize_dynamut2_ddg` (DynaMut2 reports positive=STABILISING вЂ” OPPOSITE; `DYNAMUT2_DDG_SIGN`=в€’1). **Empirical fallbacks are EXCLUDED** from the dynamics axis (a BLOSUM/B-factor estimate is not dynamics в†’ not_computed). Reuses the author-resnum identity + chain-aware key (round-trips cleanly; no SSM alignment needed). Live-verified: all 4 axes present on one residue (1-start + non-1-start), sign correct on buried L99 (+1.9 destabilising), API failure в†’ deep completes. |

(U) **Usability** вЂ” behaviour matches `execute`/`clarify`/`refuse` (a confident wrong call on a clarify/refuse case FAILS; hallucinated non-registry tools FAIL anywhere). **Aggregate** = config-tunable weighted mean **A 0.50 / F 0.35 / U 0.15** (normalised over applicable dims) + a strict **fully-correct rate** (passes every applicable dim); both reported, never calibrated-to-pass. One ROW per structure Г— group; `session.alignments.new_alignment(reps, identify_as="grp_"+hash)` auto-associates ALL chains with matching sequences in ALL open models (clicking the О± row selects all О± copies вЂ” native ChimeraX). | `qt_presenter.py` | `QtPresenter`, `PresenterSignals`, `render_html()` | вњ… Complete (unified-GUI 2026-06-13) | **The GUI Presenter вЂ” the SAME engine driven from a worker thread.** OUTPUT methods render the Rich renderable to HTML **on the worker** (pure) and emit a queued Qt signal в†’ a UI-thread slot appends to the pane (widgets never touched off the UI thread; Rich styles в†’ coloured HTML via `export_html`). BLOCKING input methods emit a signal to show the prompt then **block the worker on a `queue.Queue`**; the UI thread stays live and, on the user's answer, puts the value in the queue в†’ the worker unblocks. This worker-block pattern is what makes the straight-line engine work on a thread with no resumable state machine. |
| `gui_app.py` | `StructureBotWindow`, `ManagedService`, `_RequestWorker`, `_ToolRequestWorker`, `_PreflightWorker`, `_LoadModelWorker`, `_HistoryLineEdit`, `show_model()`, `_on_tool_launch()`, `main()` | вњ… Complete (unified-GUI 2026-06-13; S3b panel-launch wiring 2026-06-14; sequence-favored splitter 2026-06-17) | **The default front-end (== the engine host).** **Layout (2026-06-17):** the workbenchв†”console divider is a vertical `QSplitter` defaulting **sequence-favored 3:2** (workbench majority, via `setSizes`+stretch factors) instead of the old console-favored 2:3; the user's drag is persisted via `QSettings("StructureBot","StructureBot")` `ui/splitState` (`saveState` in `closeEvent`, `restoreState` in `_build_ui`, 3:2 fallback). **S3b:** `workbench.launchRequested` в†’ `_on_tool_launch(spec)` runs the panel-built spec on a `_ToolRequestWorker` (QThreadPool) via `engine.handle_tool_request` with the SAME `QtPresenter` (so the confirm-gate uses the real GUI confirm dialog + cancel/in-flight machinery вЂ” one engine request at a time); on `done` it fires the S3a consume path (`workbench._import_mpnn` / `_load_suggestions`) so results auto-render. **S4a:** for `refresh="stability"` the worker passes an `on_result` capture into `handle_tool_request`; `_on_tool_done` hands the captured result to `workbench.apply_stability_result(variant_id, result)`. Constructs the four collaborators (translator/ToolRouter/SessionState + bridge; other bridges lazy in ToolRouter) + a `QtPresenter` + `RequestEngine(self)`; sequence-model tabs over a conversation pane + a `_HistoryLineEdit` (в†‘/в†“ recall); a request runs on `_RequestWorker` (QThreadPool вЂ” long ops off-thread by virtue of running there). **Self-launching preflight** (`_PreflightWorker`): detect/launch ChimeraX REST + ping; detect/start Ollama via a `ManagedService` (detached/windowless/logged, bound to the configured host:port via `OLLAMA_HOST`); WSL/Rosetta; GUI restore prompt; API-key DEGRADE (no exit). **`confirm`** в†’ a QMessageBox with Execute/Edit/Cancel + a QTimer auto-clicking Execute on timeout (the msvcrt-countdown analog). **Cancel** в†’ clean abort at a prompt, or KeyboardInterrupt injection mid-run в†’ the engine's snapshot-restore. **Ground-truth tab focus** via the bridge's `on_structure_opened` hook (real `_opened_model_id`; `next_model_id()` the fallback) в†’ `show_model`/`_on_model_loaded`/`_focus_model`/`_LoadModelWorker` + `controller.load_model` (the seq-editor view pieces, ported in). **Teardown** (closeEvent): saves `session.json` + stops the Ollama it started; ChimeraX is left running (the user's viewer). |
| `seq_library.py` | `sequence_group_key()`, `ChainGroup`, `group_chains_by_sequence()`; re-exports `chain_resnum_to_seqpos`, `build_numbering_header_content` | вњ… Complete (variant-workbench S1, 2026-06-14) | **Pure (no Qt/ChimeraX) sequence helpers shared by the in-process Qt surfaces (seq_editor grid + the Variant-Design Workbench).** Re-exports the existing pure spine (one copy each): the resnumв†’1-based column map and the ruler builder (the ChimeraX-native `numbering_header_command` calls the SAME ruler fn вЂ” a true shared call). NEW: `group_chains_by_sequence` collapses homo-oligomer copies into one group ("edits apply to all copies"); `sequence_group_key = (md5(seq)[:12], sorted-resnums)`. **BOUNDARY (honest):** `sequence_viewer.consolidated_viewers_command` runs its grouping inside a RUNSCRIPT and can't import this across the process boundary вЂ” it uses the IDENTICAL key inline, PINNED equal by `tests/test_seq_library.py` so they can't drift. |
| `variant_model.py` | `Variant`, `ChainDesign`, `DesignSession`, `AlignedCell`, `Mutation`, `ResultSlots`; `build_design_session()`, `build_design_session_from_sequence()`, `column_tracks()`, `import_mpnn_designs()`, `build_color_commands()`, `build_color_commands_by_resnum()`, `filter_new_mpnn_variants()`, `group_scan_suggestions()`, `suggestion_color()`, `candidate_ddg()`, `stability_summary()`, `fold_summary()`; `ChainDesign.add_variant/edit_variant/get_variant` | вњ… Complete (variant-workbench S1+S2+S3a+S4a+S4b+S4c; de-novo Stage 1, 2026-06-20) | **Pure data model for the Workbench (no Qt/ChimeraX; fully mock-testable).** A generalization of `seq_editor.ChainSeq` (ONE overlay) to N named variant rows per UNIQUE chain on a shared COLUMN axis. Two PRE-SHAPES: (a) MPNN designs в†’ parallel variant rows w/ provenance (`import_mpnn_designs`); (b) every cell is residue-OR-gap (indels DONE 2026-06-18 вЂ” `delete_variant_residue`/`insert_variant_residues`/`remove_variant_insertion` + `IndelEvent`; the column axis is the indel-aware correspondence via `build_fold_column_map`). `column_tracks` = consensus + conservation. **S2:** `add_variant` (aligned COPY of T with FRESH AlignedCells вЂ” no bleed into T/siblings), `edit_variant` (lossless vs T, **revert-on-equal**, gap/non-standard-aa guarded, T immutable), `build_color_commands(cells, members, color_for)` (run-grouped `color #M/C:resnums hex` over ALL copies + white baseline, generalizes `camsol_bridge._build_viz_commands`, decoupled from the registry). Persisted via `session_state.design_sessions` (`to_dict`/`from_dict`). **S4a result helpers (pure):** `candidate_ddg` (best ddG axis: Rosetta>ThermoMPNN>RaSP) В· `stability_summary` (scan candidates в†’ per-resnum ddG + ОЈddG + rows, matched to the variant's OWN (resnum,to_aa) so only the designed subs are attributed) В· `build_color_commands_by_resnum` (per-residue-VALUE analog of build_color_commands for the ddG result mode вЂ” baseline reset + run-grouped per-resnum hex over all copies). `ResultSlots` (fold/stability/solubility/scans) filled by the panel. **S4c:** `ChainDesign.wt_refs[f"{engine}:{target}"]` (per-combo seed-pinned WT reference fold + per-residue floor, persisted) + `build_model_color_commands` (colours the PREDICTED variant model `#mid/<chain>` in its own numbering, real folded atoms вЂ” not the crystal backbone) + `fold_summary` now also carries `target`. **Row-delete (2026-06-17):** `ChainDesign.delete_variant(variant_id)` removes a variant ROW + its `ResultSlots` only вЂ” never touches `template_cells` (numbering), siblings, or `wt_refs`. **Indel Stage A вЂ” residue DELETION (2026-06-18):** `IndelEvent` (distinct from a substitution `Mutation`; persisted) + `ChainDesign.delete_variant_residue` (cellв†’gap + event, drops the substitution there; guarded) / `restore_variant_residue` (rebuild from template вЂ” lossless) + `build_fold_column_map(variant, template_cells)` в†’ `{variant_fold_resnum: reference_fold_resnum}` pairing the two folds by COLUMN (identity for substitution-only; shifts to template pos+1 after a deletion; deleted column absent). Insertion = Stage B (grows the shared axis). **S4b fold reducer (pure):** `fold_summary(step_data, author_resnums, reference_model_id=)` в†’ the normalized engine-agnostic fold contract `{engine, model_id, mean_plddt, plddt(author-resnum-keyed), reference_model_id, rmsd, source, chain}` for `ResultSlots.fold` вЂ” remaps the engine's 1-based per-residue pLDDT onto the variant's author resnums (the predicted model's own 3D colour is numbering-agnostic via `palette alphafold`); the single contract the viz/pLDDT-colour/per-model-toggle all read, so a later engine (Boltz) populates the SAME slot (adds iptm/per-chain additively). **De-novo Stage 1 (2026-06-20):** `build_design_session_from_sequence(name, chains=[(seq,copies)])` seeds a SEQUENCE-FIRST design with no crystal (synthetic `denovo-вЂ¦` ids, 1..N numbering, chain-list for hetero-later); `DesignSession.source` ("structure"\|"sequence") + `ChainDesign.template_fold` (T's own fold, populated on construct-fold, members re-pointed syntheticв†’fold) вЂ” both round-trip. |
| `color_modes.py` | `ColorMode`, `COLOR_MODES`, `all_modes()`, `get_mode()`, `ddg_color()`, `plddt_color()`; modes `none`/`hydrophobicity`/`charge`/`cysteine`/`aromatic` | вњ… Complete (variant-workbench S2+S4a+S4b+S4c, 2026-06-16) | **The SINGLE-SOURCE color registry (pure вЂ” no Qt/ChimeraX).** **S4c:** `deviation_color(dev, floor)` вЂ” FLOOR-GATED variant-vs-WT CО± deviationв†’hex (в‰¤floor в†’ neutral/None; above в†’ fixed-Г… magnitude ramp reusing tool_router's `_DEVIATION_BUCKETS` thresholds, NOT percentiles в†’ panel==3D). **S4b:** `plddt_color(plddt)` вЂ” the result-backed per-residue pLDDTв†’hex scale, BANDED to the canonical AlphaFold palette (>90 dark-blue / 70вЂ“90 light-blue / 50вЂ“70 yellow / <50 orange) so the panel cell colour equals the predicted model's 3D `color byattribute bfactor вЂ¦ palette alphafold` for the same confidence band (panelв†”3D sync). **S4a:** `ddg_color(ddg)` вЂ” the result-backed (per-residue VALUE, not aa-keyed) diverging blueвЂ“whiteвЂ“red scale for signed ddG (positive=destabilizing), white inside В±1 kcal/mol (в‰€ method noise), saturating by В±2.5; used by BOTH the panel cells (`set_result_coloring`) and the 3D (`build_color_commands_by_resnum`) so the result mode shares one source like the aa-modes. One `aaв†’hex\|None` fn per mode, used by BOTH the panel cells AND the 3D push (`variant_model.build_color_commands`) so they cannot drift. Sequence-derivable from residue IDENTITY only (NO tools вЂ” S2 scope), a sequence-PROPERTY preview not a remodel: `hydrophobicity` (Kyte-Doolittle в†’ whiteв†’deep-green), `charge` (K,R strong blue В· **His its OWN weak-blue** вЂ” only partly cationic at pH 7.4 В· D,E red В· neutralв†’reset), `cysteine` (gold), `aromatic` (F/W/Y purple; His omitted). `color_forв†’None` = no opinion (gap/unknown/neutral в†’ renders as the white reset); `none` is the explicit OFF mode (non-destructive вЂ” 3D left as-is). |
| `variant_workbench.py` | `VariantWorkbenchPanel` (+ `launchRequested` signal, `scan_launch_spec`/`mpnn_launch_spec`/`stability_launch_spec`, `apply_stability_result`, `_on_test_stability`/`_on_test_solubility`), `_ChainDesignTab` (+ `rowHeaderClicked`, `badges`, `set_result_coloring`); `_MultiSelectWorker`, `_ColorWorker`; **S4c:** "Deviation vs WT" button + `deviation_launch_spec`/`apply_deviation_result` (caches `wt_ref` per combo; confirm-gate when the WT reference must be folded) + the **"Deviation vs WT" colour mode** (floor-gated panel cells + 3D `#pred` push, one source `deviation_color`); **substitute cell-menu** вЂ” right-click a variant residue в†’ Substituteв†’[20 aa]/Revert (the existing `edit_variant` path via shared `_do_substitute`/`_after_variant_edit`). **S4b:** `fold_launch_spec`/`apply_fold_result`/`_on_fold_clicked`/`_fold_engine_availability`/`fold_visibility_commands` | вњ… Complete (variant-workbench S1+S2+S3a+S3b+S4a+S4b+S4c, 2026-06-16; responsive-toolbar pass 2026-06-17) | **The Workbench PySide6 panel (first tab in the unified GUI; thin UI over `seq_editor.controller` + `seq_library` + `variant_model` + `color_modes`).** **Toolbar (2026-06-17 responsive pass):** the low-frequency controls are grouped behind two `QToolButton` InstantPopup menus вЂ” **Tools в–ѕ** (Scan / Run ProteinMPNN / Import MPNN designs / Load scan suggestions / scan-set count + Clear) and **Fold в–ѕ** (FoldвЂ¦ / Hide folds / Tile folds / **Template** + **Variant fold** overlay toggles) вЂ” so the row sheds width and the window narrows to ~content width; direct buttons kept = + Add variant В· Substitute combo+Apply В· Test stability В· Test solubility В· Deviation vs WT В· Color. Menu entries are `QAction`s on the SAME handlers (no parallel path; the toggles are checkable QActions, so `.isChecked()`/`.setChecked()`/`.setText()`/`.text()` consumers are unchanged); the scan-set count badges the Tools button (`Tools (N)`). **Visibility authority (2026-06-17 fix):** `fold_visibility_commands` is the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH for predicted-model show/hide; the pLDDT/Deviation result colour modes colour-only (no `show #mid`) so a colour push can't re-show a toggle-hidden fold. **Delete-variant (2026-06-17):** `_ChainDesignTab.rowMenuRequested` (right-click a VARIANT header; T excluded) в†’ panel `_on_row_menu`/`_delete_variant` в†’ hides the variant's fold model (HIDE not close), `ChainDesign.delete_variant`, activeв†’T, rebuild+persist (row-delete only вЂ” no renumbering). One tab per UNIQUE chain (copies collapsed), T auto-populated on open, ruler/consensus/conservation tracks, wrapped column blocks. **S1:** column-click в†’ `controller.select_residues_multi` (ONE command в†’ ALL copies). **S2:** toolbar (+ Add variant В· AA combo + Apply В· color-mode combo); cell-click sets the active row + (variant) edit target; the **ACTIVE row drives the 3D** (T by default, a selected variant takes over + recolors on edit) вЂ” a sequence-property PREVIEW on the shared backbone, not a remodeled structure (rotamers are S4). **Sync invariant** (active-row panel color == 3D residue color) holds for EVERY residue incl. neutral (white under an active mode, mirroring the 3D reset). 3D color push off the UI thread via new **`seq_editor.controller.SequenceEditorController.run_commands`** (trusted tool-viz вЂ” direct to the bridge, bypasses the free-translation emission guard, like select). **S3a (consume cached tool results):** "Import MPNN designs" reads `session.get_proteinmpnn_result` в†’ batch variant rows (provenance, dedup on fasta_path+design_k, chain-matched); "Load scan suggestions" reads `session.get_scan_result` в†’ a SPARSE inline **"Suggest" track** (top candidate per scanned column, score-colored, tooltip = ranked list); clicking a Suggest cell в†’ QMenu of ranked candidates в†’ accept into the ACTIVE variant (provenance `accepted_suggestion` + scan score). MPNN = whole rows; scanner = inline cherry-pick (joint-design honesty by construction). **S3b (LAUNCH tools from the panel):** "ScanвЂ¦" (Fast/Deep) + "Run ProteinMPNNвЂ¦" (Default/Solubility) toolbar buttons; **Ctrl(+Cmd)-click** on a residue cell TOGGLES it into the **scan set** (`_scan_cols` вЂ” the deterministic scan scope, with an "N В· Clear" label; the set is 3D-selected across all copies; reset on load/tab-change) вЂ” a DISTINCT gesture: a PLAIN click keeps its full S2 meaning (active row + edit target), so editing is unchanged (the tab reads the modifier and emits `cellClicked2(row_id, col, ctrl)`; `_on_cell(..., to_scan=ctrl)`). A click builds a deterministic launch spec via pure `scan_launch_spec(deep)` / `mpnn_launch_spec(soluble)` (tool + tool_inputs `scan_positions`/`design_positions`+`run_rosetta`/`bias_toward`, a deep scan в†’ `confidence="low"`, and a **trigger-free `user_input` label** вЂ” no "selected"/"rosetta"/"residue N" tokens the tiering would parse) and emits `launchRequested(spec)`; the window runs it through `engine.handle_tool_request` (the SAME spine), then the S3a consume path renders the results. The panel has NO engine вЂ” it only describes the request. **S4a (make a variant TESTABLE):** per-variant **Test stability** (Fast/Deep dialog в†’ `stability_launch_spec` builds a `mutation_scan` spec with `score_mutations={resnum: to_aa}` = the variant's EXACT mutations в†’ the S3b spine; deep в†’ `run_rosetta`+`confidence="low"` confirm-gate) and **Test solubility** (pure `camsol_solubility_score` О” vs T вЂ” instant, no spine) buttons act on the ACTIVE variant. Results land in `Variant.results` (`ResultSlots`): stability via the engine `on_result` seam в†’ `stability_summary` (per-resnum ddG + ОЈddG, matched to the variant's own (resnum,to_aa)), captured by the window's `_on_tool_done` в†’ `apply_stability_result` (which also snapshot+restores the shared scan cache so the S3a Suggest track survives). Inline result **badges** render in the variant row header (`_ChainDesignTab.badges`); a header click (`rowHeaderClicked`) opens an expandable per-mutation **detail** popup. New **"ddG (result)" color mode** (`_RESULT_DDG_MODE`) paints the active variant's per-residue ddG via `color_modes.ddg_color` (diverging blueвЂ“whiteвЂ“red) on rows (`set_result_coloring`) AND 3D (`build_color_commands_by_resnum`, all copies). LIVE-VERIFIED via `scripts/verify_workbench_stage2_live.py` (S2) + `scripts/verify_workbench_stage3a_live.py` (S3a) + **`scripts/verify_workbench_stage3b_live.py` (S3b вЂ” Deep gate CANCEL keeps Rosetta unlaunched; Fast scan + REAL ProteinMPNN through the real spine; accept recolors both copies, `ribbon_color` readback)** + **`scripts/verify_workbench_stage4a_live.py` (S4a вЂ” on a real 1HSG homodimer: a Deep stability spec hits the estimate+confirm-gate and CANCEL leaves ResultSlots empty; a Deep stability run through the real spine lands Rosetta ddG (+1.95/+2.74) in ResultSlots; the ddG mode's per-residue non-white diverging commands read back matching `ddg_color` in BOTH copies; solubility О” pure)**. **S4b (engine-agnostic monomer fold):** a **FoldвЂ¦** engine-picker button (B2 3-state via `_fold_engine_availability` вЂ” ESMFold enabled, Boltz shown-disabled until its stage) builds a deterministic `fold_launch_spec(engine)` (tool=engine, `open_model`+`local_only`+`compare_to`, the variant's exact sequence, `confidence="low"`в†’confirm-gate) and emits `launchRequested`; the executed result lands via the `on_result` seam в†’ `apply_fold_result` в†’ `fold_summary` into `ResultSlots.fold`. The fold OPENS a real pLDDT-coloured ChimeraX model matchmaker-overlaid on the template (`tool_router._fold_viz_commands`, the shared engine-agnostic viz). New **"pLDDT (result)" colour mode** (`_RESULT_PLDDT_MODE`): panel cells via the generic `set_result_coloring` (`plddt_color`), 3D recolours the PREDICTED model by its B-factor (`palette alphafold`). **Per-model visibility** (`fold_visibility_commands`): active-row coupling (show the active variant's model, hide the others) + a global "Hide folds" toggle. LIVE-VERIFIED via **`scripts/verify_workbench_s4b_live.py`** (real 1HSG, ESMFold on `device=cuda`: LOCAL-ONLY `source==local_venv312`, real model + matchmaker overlay + pLDDT colour, reproducible re-fold, per-model toggle). |

## 4. Configuration Reference

### ChimeraX

| Constant | Default / Current value | Description |
|----------|------------------------|-------------|
| `CHIMERAX_PATH` | `C:\Users\andre\documents\ChimeraX 1.11.1\bin\ChimeraX.exe` | Path to ChimeraX executable |
| `REST_HOST` | `"127.0.0.1"` | REST server host |
| `REST_PORT` | `60001` | REST server port |
| `REST_TIMEOUT` | `10` | Seconds per HTTP request to ChimeraX |
| `CHIMERAX_SHOW_SEQUENCE_ON_OPEN` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false` to disable) | After a successful structure open, open + associate the Sequence Viewer for the new model |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_PER_CHAIN` / `вЂ¦_MAX` | `True` / `8` | Open one Sequence Viewer **per chain** (selectable separately, not collapsed to "chains A,B"); a structure with more chains than `вЂ¦_MAX` falls back to the single grouped viewer |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_DOCK_BOTTOM` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false` to disable) | Re-dock the Sequence Viewer(s) along the **bottom** edge, stacked vertically (via the Qt dock widget вЂ” no REST command exists) |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_NUMBERING` / `вЂ¦_NUMBER_INTERVAL` | `True` / `10` | Add a residue-number **ruler** to each per-chain viewer (or consolidated group viewer), labelled every N residues with the **actual PDB resnums** (via `chain_resnum_to_seqpos`, consistent with MPNN numbering). Custom fixed header вЂ” 1.11.1's native numbering is position-based |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_CONSOLIDATE_THRESHOLD` | `3` (env `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_CONSOLIDATE_THRESHOLD=N`) | Chain count above which per-chain viewers are consolidated into ONE alignment window per unique sequence group (fixes the "N chains letterbox the 3D view" problem). 1вЂ“3 chains в†’ per-chain unchanged; 4вЂ“8 в†’ consolidated; >8 в†’ whole-model fallback. A group = all chains with the same sequence string AND residue numbering map |
| `CHIMERAX_LEAN_LAYOUT` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false`) | Apply the lean window layout once per session (hide Log / Command Line Interface / Toolbar; menubar + title bar kept) |
| `CHIMERAX_LEAN_LAYOUT_COMMANDS` | `["tool hide Log", 'tool hide "Command Line Interface"', "tool hide Toolbar"]` | The lean-layout command list (config-driven, NOT LLM, NOT `preset`); all verified live in 1.11.1 |
| `CHIMERAX_DEFAULT_PRESENTATION` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false`) | Apply the deterministic default presentation per structure open (after load, before analysis colouring) |
| `CHIMERAX_DEFAULT_PRESENTATION_COMMANDS` | `["hide solvent atoms", "cartoon", "show ligand atoms", "style ligand stick", "color bychain", "color ligand byhetero", "set bgColor black", "lighting soft", "graphics silhouettes true", "view"]` | The presentation command list; all verified live in 1.11.1. Analysis colourings (CamSol/ESM/MPNN) run later and override the by-chain baseline; SCF sequence regions still land |
| `SEQVIEW_CACHE_DIR` | `cache/seqview/` | Scratch dir for `.scf` coloring files + their `runscript` loaders (forward-slash paths) |

### Local LLM (Ollama) вЂ” translation is LOCAL-ONLY

`TRANSLATOR_BACKEND`, `TRANSLATOR_FALLBACK`, and `ANTHROPIC_MODEL` were **REMOVED (2026-06-14)** вЂ” there is no Claude/Anthropic path and no backend switch (see В§0 invariant). Translation + intent classification run unconditionally on the local Ollama model.

| Constant | Default / Current value | Description |
|----------|------------------------|-------------|
| `OLLAMA_BASE_URL` | `"http://localhost:11434"` | Ollama server base URL (the ONLY network endpoint the translate path touches) |
| `OLLAMA_MODEL` | `"qwen3:8b"` | Exact model+tag (pulled + verified for schema-constrained structured output; fits the 12 GB RTX 5070 Ti) |
| `OLLAMA_NUM_CTX` | `16384` | Context window. StructureBot's system prompt (role + rules + full ChimeraX command reference) is **~7.5k tokens**, plus the targeted few-shot вЂ” so num_ctx must be в‰Ґ~10k or Ollama **silently truncates the prompt** (model never sees the rules/few-shot в†’ routing collapses; this was the dominant cause of the D1 engineering-tool failures). 16384 fits prompt+few-shot+generation and the 8B KV cache still fits the 12 GB card. **вљ  Over-sizing BEYOND VRAM** spills to CPU вЂ” slow + degrades constrained decoding; tune to your GPU |
| `TRANSLATOR_TOOL_NAMES` | 24 router literals | Canonical lowercase tool names the router dispatches on вЂ” ENUM-constrains the Ollama backend's `tools_needed` (constrained decoding cannot emit a misspelled/hallucinated/wrong-cased tool). A test asserts it вЉ‡ the `_dispatch_tool` registry |
| `OLLAMA_KEEP_ALIVE` | `"30s"` | Idle keep-alive before Ollama unloads from VRAM. SHORT; the explicit `ensure_translator_unloaded()` is the real contract (don't rely on the timer) |
| `OLLAMA_TIMEOUT` | `180` | Per-request HTTP timeout (a cold first-call model load can be slow) |
| `MAX_CONVERSATION_HISTORY` | `6` | Rolling history pairs (turns) |
| `AUTO_PROCEED_DELAY` | `2` | Seconds before auto-executing (0 = always prompt) |

### Directories

| Constant | Default / Current value | Description |
|----------|------------------------|-------------|
| `LOG_DIR` | `<project>/logs/` | Session JSONL log files |
| `SESSION_DIR` | `<project>/sessions/` | Named session `.cxs` + `.json` files |
| `RFDIFFUSION_CACHE_DIR` | `<project>/cache/rfdiffusion/` | RFdiffusion backbone-run cache (content-hash keyed); also WSL-visible via `/mnt/c` so the WSL run writes straight into it, Windows collects (no copy-back). Pairs with `wsl_bridge.RFDIFFUSION_PYTHON` = `/home/andre/rfdiffusion_env/bin/python` |

### Stability / ddG

| Constant | Default | `.env.local` override | Description |
|----------|---------|----------------------|-------------|
| `ROSETTA_BACKEND` | `"auto"` | **`"local"`** в†ђ ACTIVE | Backend: `auto`/`dynamut2`/`empirical`/`pyrosetta`/`local` |
| `ROSETTA_LOCAL_PATH` | `""` | вЂ” | Path to Rosetta binary dir (unused; local backend uses PyRosetta via WSL2) |
| `PYROSETTA_AVAILABLE` | `False` | вЂ” | Legacy flag for direct PyRosetta import (not the WSL2 path) |
| `ROSETTA_RELAX_CACHE` | `<project>/cache/rosetta_relaxed/` | вЂ” | Cached FastRelax'd PDB files (keyed by MD5) |
| `ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS` | `True` (strip) | `false` to preserve | Strip crystallographic HOH before PyRosetta (default; validated, standard practice). Set `False` to opt into **preserve** (re-append HOH; validated only on buried-water T26A). Preserve-all-static is a Rosetta anti-pattern вЂ” proper fix = selective buried-only/movable (Build Queue В§9). Relax cache is namespaced by mode (`_wat` suffix for preserve) |
| `relax_cycles` (param, not env) | `3` | вЂ” | `_run_rosetta_local()` parameter: FastRelax cycles for the per-mutation mutant relax + symmetric WT re-relax. Default 3 = production protocol (unchanged); exposed only so the convergence diagnostic can sweep 3/5/8. Cached WT baseline relax unaffected |
| `ROSETTA_MAX_WORKERS` | `8` | e.g. `12` | Deep-tier (Rosetta) pool size вЂ” independent per-mutation FastRelax units run via `multiprocessing.Pool` inside the one WSL2 worker (FIX D). Default 8 = i9-14900HX **P-core** count; do NOT set to the 32 logical threads (E-cores ВЅ-speed, HT, single-channel DDR5, 140 W throttle). Runtime-capped by `resolve_rosetta_workers` в†’ `min(this, ROSETTA_PHYSICAL_CORESв€’2, ROSETTA_WSL_MEM_BUDGET_MB/ROSETTA_WORKER_FOOTPRINT_MB)` |
| `ROSETTA_PHYSICAL_CORES` | `os.cpu_count()` | **`24`** on this box | Physical cores for the CPU cap (leaves 2 headroom). Default is best-effort logical count; set to the true physical count (i9-14900HX = 24) |
| `ROSETTA_WSL_MEM_BUDGET_MB` | `12000` | вЂ” | WSL2 RAM the pool may use (default WSL = ~50% host = ~16 GB on 32 GB; 12 GB leaves host/Chrome headroom). Caps workers at budget Г· footprint |
| `ROSETTA_WORKER_FOOTPRINT_MB` | `1200` | вЂ” | Measured per-worker PyRosetta footprint (~1 GB on the 2HHB tetramer) + margin; the divisor for the memory cap |
| `ROSETTA_BASE_SEED` | `1` | вЂ” | Fixed base seed for `mutation_seed(base, key, traj)` в†’ deterministic, reproducible ddG AND the parallel==serial identical-results contract (ranking/sign are seed-independent regardless) |
| `ROSETTA_PER_MUT_BASE_SEC` / `_BASE_RES` / `_EXPONENT` | `10` / `46` / `1.8` | вЂ” | **Deep-tier runtime-estimate calibration (estimate-honesty fix, 2026-06-09).** `per_mutation_sec(n) = BASE_SEC Г— (n/BASE_RES)^EXP` вЂ” SUPER-linear in pose size, anchored to measured points (1CRN 46 res в‰€ 10 s/mutation; 2HHB 574 res в‰і 733 s, killed-before-finish lower bound в†’ model gives ~940 s, biased high). Replaces the old flat ~25 s/position constant that ignored pose size |
| `ROSETTA_SHORTLIST_K` | `15` | вЂ” | Deep-tier **shortlist** size вЂ” when the user opts into "shortlist", Rosetta validates the fast tier's top-K by combined score; the rest are RETAINED as `not_computed` (never dropped). FULL grid is the default; shortlist is offered (with its own estimate) when the full-grid estimate exceeds `ROSETTA_FULL_GRID_OFFER_SEC` |
| `ROSETTA_FULL_GRID_OFFER_SEC` | `300` | вЂ” | When the full-grid deep estimate exceeds this, the confirm/tier surface presents BOTH full and shortlist options with distinct estimates (data-vs-speed is an explicit choice, never silent) |
| `ROSETTA_DDG_BASIS` | `"symmetric"` | `asymmetric` | ddG basis. **symmetric** (default) = per-mutation paired WT re-relax (variance-reduced). **asymmetric** (opt-in via "asymmetric") = score each mutant against the single cached global-WT relax вЂ” ~2Г— faster, noisier, **labelled in output**; the two are never mixed in one scan |
| `ROSETTA_PARALLEL_EFF_REF_RES` | `574` | вЂ” | Estimate large-pose guard (BUILD 3): at/below this (the 2HHB anchor) the `/workers` divisor is trusted; ABOVE it, parallel efficiency = REF/n_res (<1) shrinks the effective worker count so the estimate stays BIASED HIGH for bandwidth-bound big complexes (never undershoots) |
| `ROSETTA_WORKER_BASE_MB` / `_MB_PER_RES` | `500` / `2.2` | вЂ” | **Pose-size-scaled per-worker footprint (FIX 2).** `worker_footprint_mb(n) = BASE + PER_RESГ—n` вЂ” calibrated to 2HHB (8 workers в‰€ 1.75 GB each @ 574 res в†’ ~1763 MB в‡’ cap_mem 6, not the lucky 8). `resolve_rosetta_workers` uses this so the pool shrinks for large complexes and never oversubscribes WSL into swap. `ROSETTA_WORKER_FOOTPRINT_MB` (flat 1200) is now only the fallback when pose size is unknown |

The MULTIPLE-mutation (prediction_mm) sign is only INFERRED (endpoint chronically ERRORs). **ENFORCED GUARD (not just a flag):** while False, a returned mm result is treated as **NOT_COMPUTED** вЂ” the sign-normalised mm value is NEVER emitted; the pair falls to the additive fallback (a sum of the VERIFIED single-mutant ddGs) with a surfaced warning. So even if the endpoint recovers, the inferred mm sign cannot leak into output. Set True ONLY after a live mm anti-symmetry/known-mutation check. The mm fixture sign-corrections are as provisional as this |

## 5. Critical Conventions

### Subprocess rules (wsl_bridge.py, enforced everywhere)
All subprocess calls that interact with Windows console handles **must** use:
```python
stdin=subprocess.DEVNULL
creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW
```
Rationale: `wsl.exe` calls `SetConsoleMode()` on the inherited stdin handle, which permanently disables `ReadConsole()` for the rest of the process lifetime, breaking the Rich REPL.

### Path handling rule
All file paths passed to ChimeraX commands **must** use `.as_posix()` to produce forward slashes. ChimeraX on Windows rejects backslashes in `save "..."` and `open "..."` commands.
```python
cx_fwd = Path(some_path).as_posix()
result = bridge.run_command(f'save "{cx_fwd}"')
```

### Worker script rules (ESM worker, ESMFold worker, PyRosetta worker, double mutant PyRosetta worker)
Worker scripts that run in subprocesses or WSL2 **must**:
1. Have zero imports from the StructureBot project
2. Communicate exclusively via JSON files (never stdin/stdout for structured data)
3. Write a result file even on exception (`try/except` at the outermost level)
4. Use `flush=True` on all print calls
5. PyRosetta workers: use double-braces `{{...}}` throughout (embedded in Python f-string)

### ChimeraX selector ordering rule
In ChimeraX commands, specifiers must appear in this order to avoid syntax errors:
```
#{model}/{chain}:{residue}@{atom}
```
Example: `#1/A:82@CA` вЂ” model first, then chain, then residue, then atom.

### Primary model guard
Commands that should only act on the first loaded model must use `#1` explicitly. The translator's static system prompt instructs the model to always emit `#1` for single-model operations.

### f-string double-brace rule in worker scripts
The PyRosetta and double-mutant worker scripts are embedded as Python f-strings. Any literal `{...}` that should appear in the worker code must be written as `{{...}}`. Only actual f-string interpolations from the outer scope use single braces (e.g., `{wsl_pdb!r}`, `{mut_list_json!r}`).

### Error-first return convention (all bridges)
All bridge `analyze()` methods return `ToolStepResult` вЂ” they **never raise**. On failure, `result.success = False` and `result.error` contains the message. Callers check `result.success` and degrade gracefully.

### Windows UTF-8 stdout convention (canonical fix 2026-06-07)
`tests/conftest.py` and `main.py` both call `sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")` / `sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")` guarded by `if sys.platform == "win32" and hasattr(sys.stdout, "reconfigure")`. This is the **canonical fix** вЂ” after reconfigure, all Python print() calls can freely use О±, ОІ, в†’, в‰Ґ and any Unicode character. **Do NOT degrade scientific Unicode (О±, ОІ, etc.) to ASCII.** Arrow `в†’` in display/debug strings may use `->` for brevity; Greek letters stay Unicode everywhere (data, files, console).

`console.print()` from Rich is always safe and exempt. The `_safe_print`/`_pprint` ASCII-fallback wrappers in `rosetta_bridge.py`/`disulfide_bridge.py` predate the reconfigure fix and remain as defensive fallbacks; new code should rely on the reconfigure instead.

### Double mutant mode detection (in `_run_double_mutant`)
Epitope keywords: `"epitope"`, `"binding"`, `"interface"`, `"preserve"`, `"target"` в†’ `mode = "epitope"`. Otherwise в†’ `mode = "stability"`. PyRosetta keywords: `"pyrosetta"`, `"rosetta"`, `"accurate"`, `"high accuracy"`, `"validate"` в†’ `run_pyrosetta = True`.

### Double mutant ddG / fallback semantics
- **`ddg=0.0` is neutral/unknown, not destabilising.** The stability-mode pair filter excludes a pair only when **both** mutations have `ddg > DOUBLE_MUTANT_DESTABILISING_DDG` (default +2.0 kcal/mol). A single `ddg=0.0` mutation never eliminates a pair. (Earlier logic required at least one *beneficial* mutation, which collapsed the candidate set to ~2 pairs whenever DynaMut2 returned all-zero О”О”G.)
- **Additive fallback never drops a pair.** When no epistasis-aware backend is available вЂ” DynaMut2 mm API down, circuit breaker tripped, or a close pair with `run_pyrosetta=False` вЂ” `_apply_additive_fallback()` scores the pair as `ddG_A + ddG_B` with `epistasis=0.0` and `backend_used="additive_fallback"`, and appends a warning. Set `DOUBLE_MUTANT_ADDITIVE_FALLBACK=False` to drop such pairs instead.

All WSL/ChimeraX calls mocked вЂ” no live fold in CI.

Run commands:
```bash
# Full suite (excludes slow benchmarks)
pytest tests/ --ignore=tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -q

# Including benchmark collection check
pytest tests/ -q --collect-only

# PyRosetta benchmarks (slow, requires WSL2+PyRosetta)
pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -m benchmark -v --timeout=1800 -s

# Double mutant tests only
pytest tests/test_double_mutant_bridge.py -v

# Single benchmark spot-check
pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -m benchmark -v -s -k "t4_l99a"
```

| `test_session_state.py` | 7 | Auto-restore: `try_load`/`load` robustness (corrupt/missing/non-dict JSON), scan-result round-trip, `clear session` wipe, ChimeraX presence check + re-open offer |
| `test_integration.py` | 6 | End-to-end route + execute mock (no live ChimeraX or APIs) |
| `test_chimerax_bridge.py` | 4 | Auto-reconnect: dropped-connection retry succeeds silently, clear error when reconnect fails, no reconnect on success, `run_commands` mid-list recovery |
| `test_encoding_guard.py` | 5 | **Unicode/stdout encoding regression guard**: (1) `test_stdout_encoding_is_utf8` вЂ” asserts `sys.stdout.encoding` is UTF-8 (verifies `tests/conftest.py` ran and reconfigured stdout); (2) `test_runtime_unicode_strings_encode_under_stdout_encoding` вЂ” builds runtime Greek strings (`О±`, `ОІ`, `в†’`) assembled from parts (not literals), asserts each encodes under `sys.stdout.encoding`; catches the gap the old source-scan missed (runtime-assembled strings invisible to grep); (3) `test_scope_chain_refs_print_runs_without_error` вЂ” `redirect_stdout`, calls `_scope_chain_refs_to_macromolecule` with a bare-chain-ref command, asserts `[chain-scope]` in output (no exception); (4) `test_sanitize_zone_syntax_print_runs_without_error` вЂ” same for `_sanitize_zone_syntax`; (5) `test_session_state_greek_strings_roundtrip` вЂ” puts `"О±2ОІ2"`, `"О± В· 2HHB:A,C"`, `"ОІ-globin"`, `"heterotetrameric (О±2ОІ2)"` in tool_results, saves to tmp JSON, reloads, asserts bit-exact equality. **Note:** `tests/conftest.py` (no test cases) reconfigures `sys.stdout` to UTF-8 at import time; this is the canonical fix for `UnicodeEncodeError` on Windows cp1252 stdout. |

**Skip conditions:**
- `test_rosetta_benchmark.py`: entire module skipped if `WSLBridge().is_available()` is False **or** `WSLBridge().check_pyrosetta()` is False
- `test_wsl.py`: individual tests skip if WSL2 not installed
- `test_esmfold.py`: local-path tests skip if `venv312` python not found

## 7. Validated Live Results

> Methodology note: live results here are the *ground-truth, end-to-end* evidence the **В§0 Investigation & Audit Discipline** requires (score the real post-router output, attribute by subsystem). New audit/benchmark briefs must satisfy that standard.
>
> **Calibration data point вЂ” mocks can hide a DEAD real path (2026-06-14).** The design-goal Stage-1 live-verify (real 1HSG) exposed that `cavity_bridge`'s SASA import (`Bio.PDB.ShrakeRupley`, a nonexistent module) had `_BIOPYTHON_SASA_OK` silently `False` in production вЂ” so `find_cavities` returned **0 buried в†’ 0 cavities for EVERY structure**, while its unit tests stayed green by mocking SASA. "Built + green" did not mean "live-correct"; only the live gate caught it. Post-fix (`Bio.PDB.SASA`): 1HSG chain A в†’ 24 buried residues в†’ 1 cavity. Other SASA consumers (`glycan_bridge`, `proline_bridge`, `structural_utils`) already imported `Bio.PDB.SASA` and were never affected; interface flagging uses ChimeraX `measure buriedarea`, not this path. Lesson: a unit test that mocks the very dependency a feature needs proves nothing about the live path вЂ” pair it with a live gate.

The following results have been confirmed working against **1HSG** (HIV-1 protease, PDB ID 1HSG, homodimer, chains A+B, ligand MK1):

| Feature | Validated result |
|---------|-----------------|
| **Design-goal Stage 1 вЂ” "redesign for solubility" (op-class 3, 2026-06-14)** | **Live on real 1HSG coords (ChimeraX + ProteinMPNN + ESMFold GPU).** BEFORE (current whole-chain default, soluble bias) = 42 mutations incl. **7 buried-core swaps** (`T80в†’V`, L76Y, L89H, I62Q, вЂ¦) that would destabilise the fold. AFTER (op-class, solvent-exposed-only at SASA в‰Ґ 40 Г…ВІ) = 30 mutations, **ALL exposed, 0 buried-core swaps** (T80 SASA 25.3 в†’ fixed); **CamSol 0.326 в†’ 1.036 (+0.709)**, ESMFold mean pLDDT 74 (MODERATE вЂ” confirms a plausible fold, not the same backbone; the honest same-backbone readout is validate-design's ESMFold+Kabsch RMSD, queued).
