### Ollama (local translation LLM вЂ” Blackwell-pinned)

| Item | Requirement |
|------|-------------|
| Binary | **Ollama в‰Ґ 0.30.0** (the Blackwell/sm_120 GPU floor). Install via the **direct download from https://ollama.com/download** вЂ” NOT an unpinned `winget install ollama`, which served a stale **0.24.0** that silently ran qwen3 on CPU while reading as "connected." The GUI's managed-service launches whatever `ollama` is on PATH. |
| Model | `qwen3:8b` вЂ” `ollama pull qwen3:8b` (translation + intent classification; fits the RTX 5070 Ti) |
| GPU placement check | **"up" в‰  "on the GPU."** Don't trust `/api/tags` reachability alone: the GUI preflight warm-loads the model then reads `/api/ps` `size_vram>0` and WARNs on CPU (mirrors `esm_bridge`'s real-kernel check). CLI: `ollama ps` (VRAM/processor column) after one generate. |
| Version floor | The GUI preflight parses `ollama --version` and warns below 0.30.0 вЂ” catches a downgrade re-introducing the 0.24-class bug. |

**Blackwell/sm_120 dependency floor (RTX 5070 Ti):** alongside torch (cu128) / dgl (`CUDA_ARCH_BIN=120`) / the colabfold jax stack, **Ollama must be в‰Ґ 0.30.0**. Older builds lack Blackwell GPU support and fall to CPU silently. The main venv's torch must be **`+cpu`** (a cu126/non-cu128 build can't run sm_120 and lies via `is_available()`); GPU torch lives only in venv312/rfdiffusion_env (cu128).

### Not pip-installable (must clone and configure)

| Tool | Setup | Config |
|------|-------|--------|
| ProteinMPNN | `git clone https://github.com/dauparas/ProteinMPNN` | `PROTEINMPNN_DIR=C:\Users\andre\documents\structurebot\ProteinMPNN` |
| RFdiffusion | `git clone https://github.com/RosettaCommons/RFdiffusion` + weights вЂ” **вњ… cloned to WSL `~/RFdiffusion`, env built 2026-06-12 (see "RFdiffusion env" below)** | WSL-clone route: `RFDIFFUSION_DIR` left unset в†’ auto-probe via `RFDIFFUSION_PYTHON` |
| **ThermoMPNN** (INSTALLED 2026-06-09) | `git clone https://github.com/Kuhlman-Lab/ThermoMPNN.git ThermoMPNN_repo` (gitignored; weights bundled in-repo вЂ” `models/thermoMPNN_default.pt` + `vanilla_model_weights/`, no external download). Then **edit `ThermoMPNN_repo/local.yaml`** в†’ set `platform.thermompnn_dir:` to the repo's ABSOLUTE path (forward slashes) so it finds the bundled ProteinMPNN weights. Deps into **venv312** (reuses the GPU env; does NOT touch torch): `venv312/Scripts/python.exe -m pip install "pytorch-lightning>=2.2" omegaconf pandas biopython wandb`. Smoke-test: `cd ThermoMPNN_repo/analysis && ../../venv312/Scripts/python.exe custom_inference.py --pdb ../examples/2OCJ.pdb --chain A --model_path ../models/thermoMPNN_default.pt --out_dir <tmp>` в†’ CSV. | `THERMOMPNN_DIR=<project>/ThermoMPNN_repo`, `THERMOMPNN_PYTHON=<venv312>` |
| **RaSP** (INSTALLED 2026-06-10, **WSL2**) | All in WSL2 (NOT venv312 вЂ” would break ESM/ThermoMPNN; NOT conda вЂ” the project's "conda" envs are pip venvs). **(1)** `cd ~ && git clone https://github.com/KULL-Centre/_2022_ML-ddG-Blaabjerg.git RaSP_repo` (weights bundled: `pretrained_models/cavity` + `ds/ds_model_0..9`). **(2)** `python3 -m venv ~/rasp_env && ~/rasp_env/bin/pip install numpy pandas scipy biopython && ~/rasp_env/bin/pip install torch --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cpu && ~/rasp_env/bin/pip install openmm pdbfixer`. **(3)** compile reduce: `cd ~/RaSP_repo/src/pdb_parser_scripts && git clone https://github.com/rlabduke/reduce.git && cd reduce && make` в†’ `reduce_src/reduce`. **(4) PORT** (modern stack): in `src/pdb_parser_scripts/{clean_pdb,extract_environments}.py` `simtk.openmm`в†’`openmm`, `simtk.unit`в†’`openmm.unit`; in `extract_environments.py` `np.int`в†’`int` and the DSSP/SASA block в†’ Biopython `ShrakeRupley` (SASA is metadata, not a model input). Worker = `rasp_worker.py` (repo). Smoke/fidelity: 1PGA в†’ **Pearson 0.88 vs `data/test/Protein_G/ddG_Rosetta/ddg.csv`**. | `RASP_DIR=/home/andre/RaSP_repo`, `RASP_PYTHON=/home/andre/rasp_env/bin/python`, `RASP_WSL_DISTRO=Ubuntu-24.04` |

**foldseek (INSTALLED 2026-06-20, WSL2 вЂ” EVAL-ONLY, LOCAL-ONLY).** Used by the template-guidance calibration eval (`scripts/eval_template_guided_calibration.py::foldseek_neighbors`) for systematic structural-neighbor search (the curated US-align panel is not a safe search вЂ” it produced a search artifact that flipped a conclusion). **(1)** static AVX2 binary: `cd ~ && wget https://mmseqs.com/foldseek/foldseek-linux-avx2.tar.gz && tar xzf вЂ¦ ` в†’ `~/foldseek/bin/foldseek`. **(2)** LOCAL PDB DB (downloaded ONCE, ~6.5 GB): `cd ~/foldseek_db && ~/foldseek/bin/foldseek databases PDB pdb tmp`. **LOCAL-ONLY invariant:** `foldseek easy-search <query> ~/foldseek_db/pdb <out> <tmp> --alignment-type 1` runs FULLY LOCAL вЂ” no remote search API at query time (only the one-time DB download hits the network, like Boltz weights / our cache PDB fetches). Config: `FOLDSEEK_EXE`/`FOLDSEEK_DB`/`FOLDSEEK_WSL_DISTRO`/`FOLDSEEK_TIMEOUT`. NOT used by the shipped app.

### ColabFold env (INSTALLED 2026-05-31 вЂ” WSL2, GPU-validated)

**Decision change:** the old "venv310 (Python 3.10), shared with RFdiffusion" plan is **superseded**. ColabFold now lives in a dedicated **WSL2 Python-3.12** venv with **hermetic CUDA via pip**; RFdiffusion is a **separate** future env (decoupled).

| Package | Env | Version (exact, installed) | Purpose |
|---------|-----|----------------------------|---------|
| `colabfold` | `~/colabfold_env` (WSL2, Py 3.12.3) | **1.6.1** | AF2-quality folding; **remote MSA server** (no local MMseqs2 DBs) |
| `alphafold-colabfold` | `~/colabfold_env` | **2.3.13** | ColabFold's AlphaFold fork (pins `jax<0.6.0`) |
| `dm-haiku` | `~/colabfold_env` | **0.0.16** | AlphaFold NN modules |
| `jax` / `jaxlib` | `~/colabfold_env` | **0.5.3 / 0.5.3** | ColabFold runtime; the ColabFold-compatible jax that ALSO supports sm_120 |
| `jax-cuda12-plugin` / `-pjrt` | `~/colabfold_env` | **0.5.3 / 0.5.3** | hermetic CUDA backend (aligned to jaxlib 0.5.3) |
| NVIDIA CUDA wheels | `~/colabfold_env` | CUDA **12.9** (`nvidia-cuda-nvcc-cu12` 12.9.86), cuDNN **9.23.0.39** | pip-pulled hermetic CUDA вЂ” does NOT touch system CUDA or `pyrosetta_env` |

**GPU validated:** `jax.devices()` в†’ `[CudaDevice(id=0)]`, `device_kind="NVIDIA GeForce RTX 5070 Ti Laptop GPU"`, platform `gpu`; 2048Ві matmul runs with **no sm_120 ptxas error**. WSL2 driver **596.49 / CUDA 13.2** (`nvidia-smi`). **Reconciliation note:** `jax[cuda12]` latest is 0.10.1 (works on sm_120), but ColabFold caps `jax<0.6.0` в†’ resolves to **0.5.3**; the cuda12 plugin must be pinned to match (`pip install "jax[cuda12]==0.5.3"`) or the PJRT C-API mismatches and aborts. 0.5.3 supports sm_120, so a clean intersection exists.

### RFdiffusion env (INSTALLED 2026-06-12 вЂ” WSL2, GPU-validated on sm_120)

Built as its **own** WSL2 venv (decoupled from ColabFold/JAX, per the decision above). Native venv (NOT Docker, NOT conda), mirroring `colabfold_env`; invoked via `wsl.exe` в†’ `wsl_bridge.RFDIFFUSION_PYTHON`. Recipe basis = the `JMB-Scripts/RFdiffusion-dockerfile-nvidia-RTX5090` dependency closure replayed natively **+ the dgl arch flag JMB omits**.

| Package | Env | Version (exact, installed) | Purpose |
|---------|-----|----------------------------|---------|
| `torch` | `~/rfdiffusion_env` (WSL2, Py 3.11) | **2.11.0+cu128** | diffusion compute; `get_device_capability()==(12,0)` confirmed |
| `dgl` | `~/rfdiffusion_env` | **2.5 вЂ” built FROM SOURCE (`dmlc/dgl@3d16000`, `USE_CUDA=ON`)** | SE3-Transformer graph ops; CUDA kernels compiled for **sm_120** |
| `se3-transformer` | `~/rfdiffusion_env` | in-repo `env/SE3Transformer`, **UNMODIFIED** (`e3nn==0.3.3`) | equivariant backbone |
| adaptations | `~/rfdiffusion_env` | e3nn `o3/_wigner.py` `weights_only=False`; `numpy<2` | the ONLY two stack patches |

**THE dgl sm_120 fix (the long-pole, RESOLVED):** dgl's CUDA arch lever is `-DCUDA_ARCH_NAME=Manual -DCUDA_ARCH_BIN=120 -DCUDA_ARCH_PTX=120` (legacy `dgl_select_nvcc_arch_flags`; drives libdgl `-gencode` AND graphbolt `CUDAARCHS`) вЂ” **NOT `TORCH_CUDA_ARCH_LIST` and NOT `CMAKE_CUDA_ARCHITECTURES`**. sm_120 is absent from dgl's `dgl_known_gpu_archs` default, so without the flag it silently builds в‰¤sm_90 в†’ runtime "no kernel image" (this is precisely the gap in JMB's Dockerfile, which is why it never had a working smoke). Reproducible recipe: `docs/rfdiffusion_activation_plan.md` В§5 (AS-BUILT).

**вљ пёЏ DURABLE MACHINE STATE вЂ” `C:\Users\andre\.wslconfig` now pins WSL2 to `memory=22GB` + `swap=8GB`.** WSL's default (~15.5 GB, 50% of the 31.7 GB host) OOMs the dgl CUDA compile (`cudafe++`/`cicc` spikes). This change affects **ALL** WSL distros, persists across reboots, and is applied via `wsl --shutdown`. Any future WSL CUDA source build should ALSO cap parallelism at **`-j3`** (incl. dgl's bare `make -j` in `graphbolt`/`dgl_sparse` build.sh, which otherwise spawn 32 jobs).

Note: JAX (ColabFold) and PyTorch (RFdiffusion, `venv312`) remain in separate envs due to CUDA runtime conflicts; `pyrosetta_env` is untouched by all of the above.

RMSE/MAE roughly halve vs single-trajectory while r is unchanged (gain in magnitude, not ranking). Build-queue item 1 is fully closed.

The committed 2LZM panel numbers (RMSE 2.73, r +0.50, sign 90%) therefore again describe the **default** path. The real future fix is **selective buried-only / movable** waters (Build Queue В§9); preserve-path 2LZM re-validation is downgraded to *conditional* (only if preserve is promoted to default or made selective).
- **Benchmark-test honesty DONE (2026-05-31)**: `test_rosetta_benchmark.py` re-scoped (Build Queue В§9 item closed). Verified: non-benchmark suite **523 passed**; benchmark module collects 12 + **skips all 12 cleanly** when WSL2/PyRosetta absent (simulated by forcing `wsl_bridge._WSL_AVAILABLE_CACHE=False`); cp1252 + logic exercised offline with synthetic data. **Did NOT run the hours-long live benchmark** (on this dev machine PyRosetta IS available, so a bare `pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py` would execute it live вЂ” guard accordingly). **Immediate next is now features**: ColabFold в†’ RFdiffusion. *(Update: ColabFold env now stood up вЂ” see the ColabFold env bullet below; the `venv310` plan was superseded by a WSL2 Py-3.12 env.)*

## 13. Changelog

| Date | Tests | What changed |
|------|-------|-------------|
| 2026-06-21 | unchanged (eval increment, no tests) | eval(template-guidance): **N=2 crystal de-novo (4ORL) вЂ” REFINES the bound: the discriminator is UNLOCKING, not a structTM threshold** (`feat/template-calibration-crystal2`). 2nd crystal de-novo design (4ORL, X-ray, 108 aa, VERY hard unguided TM 0.464) with a GAP-densified foldseek ladder (gap rungs 4Q53 .90 / 4OUQ .94 seq-id .66; structure-only 6UAE .78 / 6W3G .75 seq-id .17). Identical control rescues +0.45 (в†’0.914), the 0.90/0.94 rungs +0.42/+0.43 вЂ” BUT all by COPYING (TM_G в‰€ template's structTM-to-truth, e.g. 4Q53 TM_G 0.887 в‰¤ .90), NEVER unlocking; structure-only rungs give little (6UAE +0.11 partial, 6W3G ~0). **Across all targets the natural-vs-de-novo signature is UNLOCKING (divergent template в†’ TM_G в‰« its own structTM-to-truth): CspB (natural) 1SRO .65 в†’ TM_G 0.96 в‰« .65 = UNLOCK; both de-novo targets (6W3D, 4ORL) в†’ TM_G в‰¤ template = COPY only.** REFINED NET (N=2, confound-free): natural sequences UNLOCK from a rough ~0.65 homolog (model knows the fold); de-novo designs NEVER unlock вЂ” only COPY a ~0.90+ near-correct template, which doesn't exist for a novel design в†’ template-guidance cannot rescue a true de-novo target. Copying в‰  rescue. The unlocking test is the robust discriminator, cleaner than a structTM threshold. |
| 2026-06-20 | unchanged (eval increment, no tests) | eval(template-guidance): **CRYSTAL de-risk вЂ” DECISIVE (3rd flip): de-novo designs are NOT rescued by structure-only neighbors; the 2KL8 +0.072 was an NMR artifact** (`feat/template-calibration-crystal`). Ran a CRYSTAL de-novo design (6W3D = Rosetta "RD1NTF2_05", X-ray, 116 aa; unguided TM-to-truth 0.765) with a foldseek ladder вЂ” removing BOTH confounds (NMR ceiling + curated panel). **Identical-control rescues LARGE +0.186 (в†’0.950)** = uncompressed crystal range confirmed (vs 2KL8 NMR +0.086в†’0.858, so the NMR-compression hypothesis is TRUE at the ceiling). **BUT every non-identical neighbor gives О”Acc ~0** (6W3F .79 в†’ +0.022; 5IEP .74/seqid.13 structure-only в†’ +0.015; 6W3G .72 в†’ +0.002) вЂ” no unlock, even >0.7 structure-only. **Clean contrast: CspB (natural) unlocks from a 0.65 homolog (+0.22); 6W3D (de-novo) doesn't unlock even from 0.79 вЂ” de-novo threshold >0.79 (near-identical), natural ~0.65.** So the foldseek-era "de-novo rescues" was the 2KL8 NMR artifact. **RE-CORRECTED NET (cleanest method): template-guidance rescues NATURAL underdetermined sequences, NOT de-novo/designed targets (basin reachable only by a near-identical template, which doesn't exist for a novel design) вЂ” re-establishes the de-novo bound confound-free.** The asymmetric lesson is SATISFIED (this NEGATIVE claim used a foldseek search that CONFIRMED >0.7 neighbors exist and tested them). | 2026-06-18 | **1743 / 26 skipped / 0 failed** (live-verified) | refactor(variant-deviation): **deviation metric reworked вЂ” CО±-RMSD/Kabsch в†’ superposition-free dRMSD + CО±-lDDT, 3-tier paint** (`feat/variant-indel-insertion`). The Stage-A/B "deviation vs WT" used a global rigid-core Kabsch (`_auto_anchor_resnums`+`_anchor_kabsch`); its iterative prune locked onto a TINY core (~27/99 on a disruptive insertion), mislocalizing the per-residue shift to the lever-arm extremes (max 29 Г…) while the perturbation site read в‰€0, and the **noise floor inherited the same flaw** (cross-seed displacement floors of 10вЂ“15 Г… gated real signal to white). **Replaced** with two SUPERPOSITION-FREE per-residue signals over the indel-paired residues: **dRMSD** (`_per_residue_ddm`, all-pairs distance-RMSD, Г… вЂ” the PAINTED magnitude; rigid-body-invariant, so a whole-body move reads 0, a rigidly-displaced-but-intact element lights up) and **CО±-lDDT** (`_per_residue_lddt`, Mariani-2013 local-distance-difference вЂ” secondary, distinguishes MELTED from merely DISPLACED). **3-tier colour** (`color_modes.combined_disruption_color`, one source for panel cells + 3D `#pred`): **white** = aligned (dRMSD в‰¤ 0.5 Г…) В· **grey `#8a8f99`** = distinct from the template but within the WT reference's own cross-seed noise (not a confident effect) В· **coolв†’hot ramp** (1/2.5/5/8 Г…) = CONFIDENT disruption (dRMSD > floor_ddm **OR** lDDT < floor_lddt). Floors are now superposition-free + per-residue: `floor_ddm` = cross-seed MAX dRMSD (в‰Ґ global min `_DDM_FLOOR_MIN_A` 0.5); `floor_lddt` = cross-seed MIN lDDT (в‰¤ `_LDDT_NEUTRAL_CAP` 0.9); deterministic engine (ESMFold) в†’ floors collapse to the caps. **Reference note:** the colour is variant-fold-vs-WT-*fold* (same engine в†’ Boltz quirks cancel), while the 3D overlays on the *crystal* вЂ” "far from the crystal" в‰  what the metric measures. **HONEST LIMITS (for review):** the tier thresholds are HEURISTIC/tunable (dRMSD bands 1/2.5/5/8 Г…, aligned cut 0.5 Г…, lDDT cap 0.9), calibrated by live visual spread, NOT derived from a statistical model; validated by INVARIANT unit tests (identicalв†’0, whole-body rigid moveв†’0, a rigidly-displaced block lights up dRMSD while lDDT stays ~1, single-residue distortion drops lDDT locally) + LIVE VISUAL confirmation on real 1HSG (Boltz monomer) вЂ” **no quantitative benchmark vs the prior metric**. The old CО±-RMSD/Kabsch path + its diagnostic fields are STRIPPED; the conformer-comparison use of the anchor methods is untouched; the column-pairing + floor-gating regression coverage was MIGRATED (re-stated in dRMSD/lDDT terms, not dropped), and `verify_workbench_s4c_live.py` updated to the new contract. Per-residue click readout retained (`refN: dRMSD x/floor y, lDDT z/floor w в†’ tier`). |

| 2026-06-06 | 827 (807вњ“/20s) | fix(translator+main): **a Claude usage-cap (400) no longer crashes the REPL.** Bug from real use: with `TRANSLATOR_BACKEND=claude` and the Anthropic key over its spend cap, `open 1hsg` crashed the whole REPL with an uncaught `anthropic.BadRequestError` ("You have reached your specified API usage limits вЂ¦"). Config: `TRANSLATOR_FALLBACK`, `OLLAMA_BASE_URL/MODEL/NUM_CTX/KEEP_ALIVE/TIMEOUT` (num_ctx VRAM-spill warning documented). **Model chosen: `qwen3:8b`** (pulled + verified, 6.6 GB, fits the 12 GB RTX 5070 Ti). **Live-verified**: forced-ollama simple prompts в†’ clean runnable ChimeraX commands (0 errors, ~7вЂ“11 s); `ollama ps` resident after translate в†’ empty after `ensure_translator_unloaded`; claude-unreachable в†’ fell back to Ollama and translated; forced-ollama-down в†’ error surfaced, Claude never called. Quality caveat: the local 8B is rougher than Claude on complex prompts (the benchmark signal). **Default UNCHANGED** (`TRANSLATOR_BACKEND="claude"`); +12 in `tests/test_ollama_backend.py` (all mocked); full non-benchmark suite **680 passed + 2 skipped** (was 668; +12 added only, no existing test changed). | 2026-06-01 | 645 (626вњ“/19s) | fix(translator): **stop over-eager "flagged by the API safety filter" rejections of benign design requests** (`fix/translator-false-refusals`). Mechanism = (b): not StructureBot's own filter вЂ” `translator._call_api` raised `RefusalError` whenever the Claude translation call returned empty `content`, and `main._handle_request` framed ANY such case as a safety filter with an opaque, epitope-specific rephrasing hint and NO retry. So a single transient/over-eager empty response (e.g. on "redesign the dimer interface residues to be hydrophilic, no cysteines") blocked the request, while a near-identical phrasing passed. Fixes: (1) **one automatic retry** in `_call_api` вЂ” re-issuing the identical request typically succeeds, since the decline is non-deterministic; (2) **system-prompt SCOPE framing** in `_STATIC_SYSTEM` вЂ” routine protein-engineering (interface/dimer redesign, hydrophilic/charged substitutions, excluding/introducing cysteines, stabilising mutations, epitope mapping) is declared STANDARD structural biology that must be translated, not declined; (3) **transparent message** вЂ” on a genuine decline (after retry) the real `stop_reason` is surfaced via `_report_translation_decline`, not a generic "safety filter" assumption (main.py now catches `RefusalError` by type + the legacy message pattern).
